Initiated by London and Tokyo: Anglo-Japanese Compromise Movement 23

Naval Issue Negotiations to Begin This Autumn; British Side Denies Discussing General Outstanding Issues 24

(Tokyo) Jiji Shimpo has learned that the British government suggested to the Japanese government holding Anglo-Japanese local talks to resolve outstanding issues in East Asia. This proposal was made to Matsudaira, the Japanese ambassador to the UK, who is currently on leave in Japan. The British suggested that this meeting should be held in Tokyo in the autumn. (Reuters, 8th)

(Tokyo) An official at the British Embassy in Tokyo told a Reuters reporter today that they were unaware of any British proposal to hold Anglo-Japanese talks. They do not believe the news reported by Jiji Shimpo. (Reuters, 8th)

(London) The report carried today by the Tokyo Jiji Shinpo that the British suggested holding Anglo-Japanese talks in Tokyo this autumn to discuss Far Eastern matters has been denied by London. However, it is said that both sides may begin consultations on naval and other issues this autumn through ordinary diplomatic channels. (Reuters, 8th)

(London) The suggestion circulating in Tokyo that the UK and Japan will hold a meeting this autumn to discuss Anglo-Japanese relations worldwide, including the Far East issue, is quite welcome here. This statement cannot currently be verified. It has been heard that the Japanese ambassador to the UK, Matsudaira, returned home in July to seek a better understanding between the two countries. Public opinion believes that the import quotas imposed by British colonies could be used by the British government in negotiations to deal with Japan. An investigation shows that in the first six months of 1934, the amount of Japanese rayon fabrics imported into Sierra Leone was 255,141 yards. Imports have decreased greatly in the first six months of this year, almost to nothing. Furthermore, the complex situation in Inner and Outer Mongolia will have possible repercussions on Russo-Japanese relations. Public opinion feels that this matter will have an important relationship with the overall situation. The public also believes that Japan's national expenditures have greatly increased and that huge loans are constantly needed to balance its budget, which can restrain the activities of ambitious people. With the current coolness of Chinese sentiment towards Britain, Britain will be cautious to avoid any indication of uniting with Japan to reject China. However, Japan's position is now clearly not to be insulted, so to restore harmony, Japan's cooperation is necessary. However, assistance can be given to China in material terms. China's need for this assistance has been recognized with sympathy by the general public. (Reuters, 8th)

(Tokyo) Foreign Minister Hirota is proceeding with concrete measures to establish a lasting and friendly relationship between China and England based on the report of Ambassador Matsudaira to the UK. However, this plan requires the active cooperation of the UK. That is, the UK, recognizing Japan's position in East Asia and realizing that Anglo-Japanese cooperation can only maintain British interests in the Far East, should actively cooperate with Japan's naval disarmament proposal to ensure the success of the agreement. If the UK hopes to establish friendly Anglo-Japanese relations, it should immediately abolish the economic alliance of boycotting Japanese goods in its own country and colonies. (Domei, 8th)

(Tokyo) According to Japanese sources, Foreign Minister Hirota is determined to find a way to adjust commercial relations between the UK and Japan. The British government's plan to reject trade between Japan and British colonies, such as abolishing the Indo-Japanese Commercial Treaty of 1905 and increasing import taxes on Japanese cotton fabrics in India, is almost a fatal blow to Japan. If the UK wishes to cultivate amicable relations with Japan, it should develop a generous economic policy towards Japan. This is said to be the only way to unite friendship. Furthermore, Jiji Shinpo stated that if the UK formally recognizes Japan's power in East Asia and reconsiders events between the UK and Japan, a satisfactory resolution can be reached, which will have a good influence on naval negotiations between the two countries. The newspaper also claimed that the proposal for Anglo-Japanese talks clearly prevents the failure of the London Naval Conference. The UK, after Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations, has achieved rapid economic progress worldwide, which is greatly alarmed. It deeply feels that to maintain peace in East Asia, Japan's cooperation cannot be ignored. Therefore, before Ambassador O'Neill left London to return home, he discussed with him the suggestion that he convey to Foreign Minister Hirota a sincere discussion between the UK and Japan on commercial matters and issues related to China. The Foreign Minister now intends to accept it. Japan hopes that the British ambassador to China and Sir Frederick Leith-Ross, the economic advisor to the British government, can represent the UK at the meeting. The newspaper concluded by saying that Sir Miles Lampson, the British Ambassador to China, has tentatively agreed to the request to attend. (Reuters, 8th)

Sir Frederick Leith-Ross Comes to China; New British Policy Begins; London Newspapers Attach Importance 26

(London) Today, all newspapers reported that Sir Frederick Leith-Ross, the government's chief economic advisor, will be going to China. Sir Frederick Leith-Ross has been resting in the countryside in recent days and will not return to London until the eve of his departure by ship. He does not see reporters but speaks with those familiar with the Far East situation. He never expresses his own opinions because he has no preconceptions and will only be able to express them after arriving in China in person. Those in all circles related to China believe that the Far Eastern issue is primarily psychological. To formulate a practical plan to assist China, it must be based on the restoration of trust and goodwill between China and Japan. Sir Frederick Leith-Ross will take the Empress of Britain to Canada on August 10 and then take the Empress of Asia to China on August 22. He will pass through Japan and will visit Tokyo for a few days. (Reuters, 8th)

Comparison of British and Japanese Spindles; Japan's Total Number of Spindles Exceeds 10 Million; Britain Currently Has 45 Million 27

Osaka According to a survey by the Federation of Textile Associations, as of the end of July this year, the spindles of various spinning mills that have joined the federation totaled 9,812,000. If the 220,000 spindles of the ten mills outside the association are included, the number of spindles installed in all spinning mills in Japan exceeds 10 million. The plan for increasing spindles in the future is expected to be 600,000 this year, 650,000 next year, and 750,000 the year after that. The total number of spindles in British needle factories is currently 45 million, of which 10 million are said to be abandoned. (Dentsu, 8th)

(Tokyo) The issue of a new trade treaty between Japan and Egypt is focused on the issues of Japanese cotton cloth and Egyptian cotton. Therefore, they request that the diplomatic authorities adopt a tough approach in negotiating the new treaty and be sure to avoid adopting a quota system. (Dentsu, 8th)

US Navy Department Actively Engaged in Shipbuilding and Decides to Replenish and Replace Old Ships; Britain Also Plans to Build Ships This Year 28

(Washington) The Navy Department today opened bids for private shipyards to build one light cruiser, one aircraft carrier, eight destroyers, and three submarines. It is reported that bids will also be opened soon for eleven warships to be built in government shipyards. After this project is completed, the US Navy's aircraft carriers and cruisers will have reached the treaty limit. Destroyers and submarines will still be 54 short. A spokesman for the Navy Department reiterated today that the Navy Department has decided to replenish and replace warships that are too old. Therefore, by the end of 1936, seven battleships will be built. However, construction may be temporarily suspended until Japan's intentions are determined. (National News Agency, 7th)

(Washington) The Navy Department has decided to build 24 new battleships, of which 13 will be opened for bidding tomorrow morning by private manufacturers, and the remaining 11 will be built in state-owned shipyards. Their total tonnage is 63,000 tons. According to the new ships that the United States has planned to build in order to reach the treaty limit, 62 ships have been started, totaling 220,500 tons. Added to the existing 710,055 tons of warships within the age limit and the tonnage of the new ships to be built this time, the total is 1,000,555 tons. According to the latest news, the total tonnage of the British Navy as of this year is 1,121,393 tons. Therefore, the difference between the US and British navies is only 121,000 tons, meaning that the United States is only less than Britain by this much. Two years ago, the total tonnage of the US Navy (including new ships) was 239,800 tons less than that of Britain, and the number of ships was 102 less than that of Britain. Now, there are only 52 ships less, all of which are destroyers and submarines, including 26 destroyers and 18 submarines. After these numbers are replenished, the navies of the UK and the US will be completely equal. The 12 ships that the Navy Department has now decided to bid for construction are: (1) one 25,000-ton aircraft carrier to replace the current Langley carrier, which is only used for testing; (2) three 1,800-ton destroyers; (3) five 1,500-ton destroyers; (4) five 1,330-ton submarines. As for the 11 ships to be built at the Navy Department's shipyard, they are: (1) one 1,500-ton light cruiser; (1) seven 1,500-ton destroyers; (3) two 1,330-ton submarines. (National News Agency, 7th)

Quincy, USA A fire suddenly broke out in the radio room of the new cruiser Quincy, causing losses of approximately US$100,000. The Secretary of the Navy does not want to criticize the cause of the fire or the talk of a relationship with negligence, pending a detailed investigation. (National News Agency, 7th)

(Washington) Secretary of War Dern said today after visiting President Roosevelt that he will represent the President and go to Manila to attend the inauguration ceremony of the Philippine Commonwealth government on November 5.

(London) According to British naval expert Bywater in the Daily Telegraph, the British government plans to build warships within this year, including four built by national shipyards and 19 built by private shipyards. As for the increase in the number of cruiser crew members and the replacement procedure for old warships of all classes, it will begin soon. (Havas, 8th)

US-Philippine Cooperation to Boycott Japanese Cotton Cloth; Japanese Consul Reports to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs; US-Philippine Trade Association Plans to Boycott Japanese Goods 29

(Nanjing) Kimura, the Japanese Consul General in Manila, recently reported to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs on the relationship between Japan and the Philippines. The report stated that the US-Philippine Trade Association had published the situation of cotton cloth trade between Japan and the United States in the Philippines, intending to raise tariffs on Japanese goods and promote a boycott movement. According to the report, the Philippine Department of Agriculture and Commerce announced that the amount of Japanese cotton cloth imported into the Philippines in 1934 was 56,356,982 square meters, while American cotton cloth was only 43,410,603 square meters. Compared to the situation in 1933, Japan's advantage has greatly increased. Therefore, Japan has now taken the position of the United States as the largest cotton cloth exporter to the Philippines. Therefore, to protect the essence of Philippine industry and establish the principle of reciprocity in US-Philippine trade, it is currently an urgent issue to take measures to protect American goods. (China United Press, 8th)

US Democratic Party Suffers First Setback in Election; Republican Party Wins in Rhode Island 32

(Washington) The political trend in the United States shifts with the hearts of the people in Maine. Therefore, to know the evolution of the political situation in the United States today, one can consult Maine. In the special congressional election held in Rhode Island yesterday, Republican candidate Risk, with the slogan of defeating Roosevelt, received 41,237 votes, while Democratic candidate Pullins, representing the New Deal movement, was defeated with 30,142 votes. Although President Roosevelt did not say a word about this phenomenon, it has left proponents of the New Deal stunned and at a loss. At the same time, the Republican Party is deeply convinced that it will be able to defeat Roosevelt in the 1936 presidential election, said House Minority Leader Snell. This is the starting point for the demise of the New Deal. To cover up the matter, the Democratic Party comforted itself by claiming that Rhode Island was originally a Republican stronghold, and this victory was merely a manifestation of the district returning to normalcy, which is not surprising. (National News Agency, 7th)

(Washington) After the Rhode Island election, financiers observed that the silver issue in 1936 will definitely become a bigger issue of contention between the two sides. The results of this election show that the Democratic Party's power in the northwest industrial area is gradually declining. To win the 1936 election, the Democratic Party must do its best to protect the interests of the southwest. According to general opinion today, the ten western states representing the silver faction and benefiting from the New Deal will still be the stronghold of the Democratic Party. Current Commentary

Fundraising for Disaster Relief 34

Disaster relief is like fighting a fire, referring to its urgency, while handling disaster relief lacks good plans, referring to its difficulty. I once saw the great Yangtze River flood in the 20th year of the Republic of China, with disaster victims covering the river downstream. The ladies and gentlemen of Shanghai took out their money, providing food and clothing. Many contributed enthusiastically without waiting for appeals. The spirit of compassion, empathy, and righteous action can be described as great. As a result, the disaster victims lingered and did not want to leave. It was difficult to send them away. Compared to the great drought disaster last year, the number of victims was no less than in the 20th year, but the public's enthusiasm for assistance was less than before. Is it that human feelings have changed so much between then and now? The reason for this is that there are years without disasters, and disaster relief is endless, weakening the power of attention, first. Helping with all one's might can be done once or twice, but not countless times. Constantly, strength is insufficient, and love cannot help, second. Rural areas are bankrupt, cities are declining, unable to take care of themselves, how can they take care of others, third. Now that the Yangtze River flood has just been reported as safe, the Yellow River flood has reappeared. The drought victims have not yet recovered, and the flood victims have followed one after another. The handling of disaster relief requires huge funds, and fundraising has no way to obtain goods. The disaster victims who are in the scorching sun and floodwaters, in the depths of water and fire, are wandering on the line of death, waiting for relief on the road to hunger. This situation is not tragic and devastating to the world.

It is heard that the disaster relief method has been concretely decided after six days of deliberations by the Executive Yuan. In general, the work relief part is for each affected province and city to accommodate as many disaster victims as possible in the original projects. Agricultural relief and emergency relief will be handled by the central disaster relief reserve fund of one million. An order is also issued to the provincial governments to spend two percent of the total amount of regular budget revenue each year as the disaster relief reserve fund for each province. However, even if the central government allocates huge funds, the disaster area is vast, and the number of those waiting for relief is so large that it is difficult to cover everything. Therefore, to save the disaster victims, one can only rely on the power of the public. So, how can the assistance of the public be obtained? I believe that official propaganda is essential. However, propaganda has become the end of its strength today, because everyone knows that it is propaganda for the sake of propaganda. Now, if you want to gain people's trust, you only need to focus on practical action. The so-called practical action is nothing more than giving people a common vision everywhere, not focusing on rhetoric, but being able to do it realistically and truthfully. We know that those who are in charge of disaster relief have mostly been handling disaster relief for many years and have a reputation. Or, in handling work relief, they have made remarkable achievements. However, for the sake of the disaster relief itself, for the righteousness of those who are most valuable in handling affairs, they should not be afraid to speak frankly. Because money is not wasted in vain, and real benefits are given to the people, which is the biggest principle of handling disaster relief. Making the public believe it and obtaining public support is the only condition for handling disaster relief. Both of these depend on whether the handling of affairs is appropriate or not. If those in charge of disaster relief and construction workers all have ardent emotions, pure integrity, and a spirit of hard work, then the matter will definitely be successful. On the contrary, if the evils of embezzling disaster relief, eating disaster relief, and being fat and muddled arise, and if they are shielded privately and not punished, then people's faith will be lost. Wouldn't it be difficult to follow up? We have often seen in newspapers the advertisements of various charitable organizations thanking donors. What is the content of their income and expenditure? Who has reports like credit reports? So far, there is no follow-up meeting with people in common. The donors firmly believe that the money has been donated and their hearts have been exhausted. Other things are not what they want to ask. Those who are in charge of affairs should fulfill their responsibilities and make a clear announcement. Not only should the donors know what the money they have donated is used for, but the public should also know that what they have received and spent is truly true and not false. Everyone is used for the disaster victims, so the public will naturally deepen their faith in it. If there are any actions after this, they will be happy to donate and will not be stingy. Some say that the accounts are vast and cannot be recorded. This is close to an excuse. How difficult is it to compile an accurate and concise comparison table of first-level income and expenditure? Why is it not done?

Fundraising should not have too many items. If there are too many, people may suspect that it is a fake name to collect money. It should not be complicated and harsh. If it is complicated and harsh, it is close to forced donations. It should not be used by people for propaganda. Once used, people may fear that it is not legitimate. The fundraising organization and personnel should be carefully selected. The audit of the donated items should be clear. Otherwise, evils will arise and the reputation will be lost. I have heard that those who specialize in charitable affairs all have religious beliefs. If they can develop a great wish to be compassionate and save people, setting an example with their own behavior, and widely persuading the world that benefiting others is benefiting oneself, it is expected that the results will be great. Unfortunately, in today's society, philanthropists still have many concerns and are unwilling to do it.

Henderson Calls for Meeting of Disarmament Conference Leaders; Date Set for Approximately September 13th 35

(Geneva) Henderson, Chairman of the Disarmament Conference, notified the committee members of the conference that a meeting of the leaders would be held during the first week of the League of Nations General Assembly. According to sources from the League of Nations Secretariat, the meeting is scheduled for approximately September 13th. The meeting will study the general situation and decide the scope of the General Assembly's current assistance work. (National News Agency, 7th)

German Authorities Continue to Dissolve the Stahlhelm; Anti-Jewish Movement Also Underway 36

(Berlin) The Stahlhelm (National Socialist Veterans' Association) in Greater Berlin and the provinces of Brandenburg, Pomerania, and Eastmark in the Polish Corridor were all dissolved today. Eastmark was the last stronghold of the group. The reason for its dissolution was that the group was engaged in activities harmful to the country and contained many people who embraced Marxism. (Reuters, 8th)

(Berlin) The cities of Gladbeck and Blö are also passed a law today, prohibiting Jewish people to go to Aryan people's schools, buy properties or go to public bathrooms and stadiums and other place. This action is practically barring the Jewish people entirely. At the same time, the official publication of the Stahlhelm party has also been banned. (National News Agency, 7th)

(Berlin) Anti-Jewish violence continues to occur here. On the gate of a certain station in the suburbs of Berlin, a wooden sign was hung, on which the words "Jews, get out!" were written in large letters. The leader of a large enterprise in Berlin prohibits members of the Labor Front from asking Jewish doctors to diagnose their illnesses. Also, two Jews were arrested by the police for riding bicycles too fast on the street. When they were arrested, the police were rude and were sentenced to one year and ten months in prison. (Havas, 8th)

Philippines; Typhoon and Heavy Rain Cause Disaster 37

(Manila) Northern and Central Luzon were struck by typhoons followed by heavy rains, resulting in vast areas being flooded and significant loss of life and property. It is reported that the number of drowned and missing people has reached 126, and the property loss is valued at 1.5 million yuan. The authorities have declared a state of emergency in the affected towns to prevent grain merchants from hoarding. At the same time, health officials are now working hard to prevent the outbreak of epidemics. (Reuters, 7th)

French Premier Meets with British and Italian Ambassadors to Prepare for Three-Nation Conference to Discuss Abyssinian Issues in Paris in Mid-Month 38

(Paris) Premier and Foreign Minister Laval met with British Ambassador to France, Clerk, and Italian Ambassador to France, Custoza, this afternoon to discuss a meeting of the three nations, Britain, France, and Italy, based on the 1906 treaty regarding Abyssinia. The conference seems to be scheduled for August 16 in Paris, but as the governments involved have yet to respond, the date has not been fully finalized. Those in charge believe that the meeting may not take the form of a formal conference, but only involve talks between British Minister Without Portfolio Eden, Mussolini's Private Secretary Aloisi, and French Premier and Foreign Minister Laval. (Havas dispatch, 7th)

(London) The three-nation conference on the Italo-Abyssinian dispute will begin in Paris on August 14 or 15. The British representative is Eden, the French representative is Premier Laval, and the Italian representative is Aloisi, who recently attended the League of Nations Executive Council meeting in Geneva. The start of the three-nation conference coincides with large-scale Italian military exercises near the Brenner Pass, a major route from Germany into Italy. Approximately one million soldiers will participate in the exercises, during which the Italian government will test new methods of assaulting enemy positions with specialized military equipment. All movements will be kept strictly secret. (Reuters dispatch, 8th)

(Paris) The tripartite Anglo-Franco-Italian conference to negotiate the Italo-Abyssinian dispute is planned to be held in Paris, pending Rome's agreement. If so, the representatives of the three countries will be able to contact Abyssinian representative Hawariat at any time, as he is the Abyssinian envoy to Paris and recently represented Abyssinia at the League of Nations Executive Council meeting. Authorities announced today that former Greek Premier Politis has agreed to be the fifth arbitrator on the conciliation committee investigating the Italo-Abyssinian case. (Reuters dispatch, 7th)

Is Rome Also Optimistic About the Paris Three-Nation Conference? Believes Agreement Between Britain and Italy is Possible 39

(Rome) People here are gradually becoming more optimistic about the Anglo-Franco-Italian conference in Paris. When the representatives of Britain, France, and Italy decided in Geneva to convene the Paris three-nation conference based on the 1906 treaty regarding Abyssinia, Italian diplomatic circles believed that the current conference could give Italy sufficient time to steer the Italo-Abyssinian issue onto a basis completely different from the League of Nations' viewpoint. However, the general public initially thought it unlikely that the British government's attitude would lead to a solution satisfactory to Italy. Now, this assessment has slightly changed. Italy has not completely given up hope of reaching a compromise with Britain, because recently some people in Britain have expressed a greater understanding of Italy's demands. According to Italian diplomatic circles, the Paris three-nation conference has not been convened immediately due to the wishes of the British side, as Britain wants to delay the opening date in order to first seek a convergence of views among the countries involved before the conference begins. The semi-official Italian newspaper, "Il Giornale d'Italia," stated that British public opinion on the Abyssinian incident can be divided into two factions: one firmly hostile to Italy, and the other acknowledging that nations other than Britain should have the right to expand their colonies. The newspaper concluded, "European peace depends on Italy's cooperation. This point was raised at the Stresa Conference. If so, then friendship between Britain and Italy will not only benefit Italy, but also benefit Britain." (Havas dispatch, 7th)

(Rome) According to political predictions, the three-nation conference on the Abyssinian issue is planned to be held in Paris on August 16. According to reports from newspapers here, the chief Italian representative will be Aloisi, accompanied by experts on African issues. It is generally believed that Britain's position at this conference will be more difficult than it was in Geneva, because in Geneva, Britain could take a stand based on League of Nations principles and morality, but here it cannot avoid making a more concrete statement. Sources familiar with the matter predict that the Italian representatives will emphasize three points: (1) Italy's past occupation of Eritrea was originally encouraged by Britain, because at that time, while America was conquering Sudan, Italy's occupation of this area could protect America's flank. (2) Although the 1906 Anglo-Franco-Italian treaty nominally aimed to maintain Abyssinia's territorial integrity, its true intention was to divide Abyssinia. (3) The 1925 exchange of notes between the three countries regarding Abyssinia, well after the establishment of the League of Nations, was actually an action to discuss the spheres of influence of the three countries in Abyssinia. Therefore, Britain has never considered itself a protector of Abyssinia. Italian officials observe that it will be difficult to erase these facts, so Britain should be able to be more realistic at this conference, and not just preach high-sounding principles. Furthermore, according to news from London, there is an increasing number of British veterans, doctors, engineers, and various craftsmen requesting the Italian embassy to allow them to join the Italian army for the conquest of Abyssinia. While the embassy expresses satisfaction with this situation, whether or not they are needed will be decided by the Italian government. (National News Agency dispatch, 8th)

Abyssinia Discloses War Plans Intends to Win Decisively in the South 40

Addis Ababa A responsible, non-official source today revealed to a Reuters correspondent Abyssinia's war plans against Italy. If this plan is adopted, the Abyssinian Emperor will not defend against the Italian army on the Eritrean or Italian Somaliland fronts. Instead, he will gather his main force near the Italian Somaliland border. When the Italian army invades Abyssinia from Eritrea, the Abyssinian Emperor will also attack from his base, hoping to win in the south and offset the losses in the north. Only a small number of troops will be stationed in the north, intending to adopt guerrilla tactics, with the sole purpose of hindering the enemy. Mobilization is progressing gradually, but continuous heavy rain makes troop movements extremely difficult. Often, a hundred-mile journey takes more than half a month to complete. The Abyssinian army's total strength is uncertain, even to the Abyssinian government. However, reliable estimates put the total number at approximately 750,000 men. They are not all equipped with modern weapons, and their organization is not entirely perfect. Many foreigners are currently volunteering for service in the Abyssinian government, but only a few experts are being recruited. 3,000 gas masks recently ordered from Germany have arrived, and another 25,000 are en route. (Reuters dispatch, 7th)

Addis Ababa According to information obtained by a Havas News Agency correspondent stationed in the capital, the Abyssinian army is divided into seven routes: (1) The Northern Route Army is commanded by Prince Siyyum, grandson of former Emperor Yohannes. (2) The Southern Route Army is commanded by Prince Desta, the Emperor's son-in-law. (3) The Central-Eastern Route Army is commanded by General Nasibu, former Governor of the capital. (4) The Western Route Army is commanded by Prince Emiru. (5) The Central-Western Route Army is commanded by Prince Kassa. (6) The Eastern Route Army is commanded by Crown Prince Asfaw Wossen. (7) There is another route, whose details are unknown. Each route army is divided into thirty regiments, with approximately 3,000 soldiers per regiment, for a total force of over 600,000 men. Of these, only 250,000 are equipped with government-issued firearms and ammunition. The total number of rifles is disputed, ranging from approximately 300,000 to 1 million. It is generally believed that Abyssinia has 200 cannons of various types, some of which are old-fashioned cannons from the 1860s. In addition, there are approximately 400 machine guns and a roughly equal number of light machine guns, as well as eight aircraft, only six of which are usable. As for the troops currently concentrated in the northern provinces, they were not mobilized by government order. Soldiers from the northern provinces believe that their provinces will bear the brunt of any conflict, so they have voluntarily joined the local commanders in those provinces to prepare to meet the enemy. (Havas dispatch, 7th)

Addis Ababa An American black aviator nicknamed "Harlem's Black Eagle" voluntarily organized an Abyssinian air force, but initially caused displeasure by damaging the aircraft during his first flight with a brand new plane. He has now regained favor, although his flying skills are not particularly impressive, as he previously served in the military training new recruits. (National News Agency dispatch, 7th)

Addis Ababa It has been learned here that the newly organized Abyssinian Red Cross has raised one million yuan in donations. (National News Agency dispatch, 7th)

Italy's 500,000-Strong Army to Conduct Autumn Maneuvers at the Brenner Pass Scheduled to Begin on August 20 41

(Rome) It was announced here today that starting August 20, a 500,000-strong army will conduct Italy's largest-ever military exercises at the Brenner Pass. The Brenner Pass is located in the foothills of the Alps and is a vital route to Austria. The plan for the exercises is being kept strictly secret. (National News Agency dispatch, 7th)

(Rome) The Italian army is currently undergoing a complete reorganization, including the General Staff. The General Staff will now establish a Staff Corps and a General Staff Department. The Staff Corps will be composed of 35 colonels and 99 lieutenant colonels. The number of personnel in the General Staff Department has not yet been determined. (National News Agency dispatch, 7th)

(Rome) Premier Mussolini has ordered all ministers and government officials concurrently holding military positions to participate in the autumn maneuvers to be held at the end of this month. Senators and congressmen are not required to participate, but those who voluntarily request to do so are exempt from this rule. (National News Agency dispatch, 8th)

Turkish Military Officer Appointed as Abyssinian Military Advisor First Chargé d'Affaires Arrives in Addis Ababa 42

Istanbul Turkish officials firmly deny reports that General Wehib Pasha has been appointed as the Commander-in-Chief of the Abyssinian army, but acknowledge that he has accepted the Abyssinian Emperor's offer to serve as a military advisor, having renounced his Turkish citizenship. It is said that he will utilize his experience from the Balkan Wars in training the Abyssinian army. (National News Agency dispatch, 8th)

Labor Strife at French Armament Factories Eases Government Changes the Scale of Pay Cuts Labor Strike Settled 43

Brest The workers at the local armament factories who went on strike in opposition to the government imposing legal mandates have restored order as of 1 AM this morning. The disorder as of yesterday was lessened in comparison to previous days, with less people attending the protests. Police are defending the city effectively and the city center was not entered by protestors. Demonstrators were singing the Internationale and shouted slogans against the police, and also threw all kinds of items, but were driven away by the police. Many of the protestors were unemployed workers and children and a few people were injured. (Havas dispatch, 8th)

(Paris) Representatives from the sailor's union met today with the shipping industry and it is widely hoped that the labor strike can be resolved. After the meeting, it was heard that the government had agreed to reduce pay cuts for a large portion of the workers from 10% to 3%. This morning, many people were going to the site of yesterday's street battles. The remains of the stalls set on fire by rioters were still smoking. This morning, workers were going in droves towards the coastline, but the armament factories had long been closed. It is heard that the armament factories will only open after the disputes have been resolved and preparations can be made. Special care must be taken this afternoon, as the workers killed in yesterday's riots will be holding their funerals. The regional governor of Brest went to inspect many locations this morning. Police were encouraged, as they had been working all day and had not been able to rest. The Atlantic Shipping Company's Champollion may be able to set sail today. The kitchen and dining room staff have returned to work, so passengers have been able to have breakfast on the ship. However, the strike leaders have said that the ship absolutely cannot set sail today. (Reuters dispatch, 8th)

(Paris) The labor strike in the shipping industry that began yesterday has now been resolved. The Champollion mail steamer will set sail for New York this evening. (Reuters dispatch, 8th)

Polish-Danzig Relations Improve Negotiations to Abolish Tariff War 44

Warsaw The recent tariff dispute between Danzig and Poland was settled today. Danzig rescinded measures adverse to Polish commerce promulgated a few days ago. Danzig also agreed to allow specific Polish goods to be freely imported into Danzig. Poland will also retract its July 18th tariff laws that placed limits on Danzig goods entering Poland. (National News Agency dispatch, 8th)

Danzig Semi-official sources have stated that relations between the Polish and Danzig governments have improved. Direct talks will begin soon, and their aim is to obtain a peace agreement to rescind the retaliatory plans that have been in effect for the past few weeks. By doing so, all disputes can be resolved. The National Socialist Party's media outlets are optimistic, saying that authorities in Warsaw and Danzig are willing to resolve outstanding cases, and that the party's policies are the same as they were in the past: solving all disputes through direct negotiation. Only if all other methods fail will the League of Nations be petitioned to solve the disputes. (National News Agency dispatch, 7th)

Danzig The Danzig Senate announced today that an accord signed on August 13th between the Free City of Danzig and the Polish government, permitting Polish warships to enter and dock in Danzig harbor, has been extended. According to the accord signed today by Danzig Senate Speaker Granzow and Polish Minister Lubieński, the term has been extended for three years. Both sides have also agreed that should either party not declare its intention to abrogate the accord within three months before its expiry, then the accord will automatically be extended for another three years. (National News Agency dispatch, 7th)

International Business Telegraph - August 8th Reuters Special Business Dispatch -

Gold and Silver

British Gold: The London gold price today was 140 shillings and 6 pence, up one penny.

British Silver: The London silver market was quiet. The spot price is 30 pence and 1875, unchanged. Futures are up 0.0625, at 30 pence and 25. American groups purchased, and India and China sold. The market closed stable.

Exchange Rates

British vs. American: The London foreign exchange market was stable this morning. Authorities are still managing the French exchange rate. The opening rate for British vs. American was 4 dollars 96 and 25 cents, the same as yesterday's closing rate for American vs. British. There were fluctuations within the first hour. It fell 0.0625 at noon, then rose 0.0625 in the next hour. At 2 PM, it rose 1875, to 4 dollars 96 and 4375 cents.

British vs. French: The opening rate was up 3 pounds sterling, at 74 francs and 93. There was no change before noon. It rose 1 pound sterling at noon. At 2 PM in the afternoon, it fell 3 pounds sterling, to 74 francs and 91.

Cotton and Wheat

American Cotton: The New York cotton market was sluggish and unremarkable before opening because the government's harvest estimate was scheduled to be released this afternoon. The general opinion is that the government's loan policy is even more important than today's estimate.

British Cotton: The Liverpool cotton market was quiet because the US Department of Agriculture report was about to be released. At 1 PM in the afternoon, the October price was 621, down 2 pounds sterling.

British Wheat: The Liverpool wheat market plummeted today because Russian wheat was once again being sold on the market. The amount currently being sold is not large, and there are no signs of dumping. At 1 PM in the afternoon, the October price fell 1 penny and 25, to 5 shillings and 2 pence.

American Wheat: The Chicago wheat market opened unchanged, and prices fluctuated unevenly.

New York commodity prices showed a slight downward trend. Reports of heavy rain in Argentina and news that Russian wheat would be sold caused the recent bullish sentiment to cool slightly, but many still believe that the current position is fundamentally favorable to bullish traders. Coarse grains were firm before noon.

Rubber

London: The London rubber market opened slightly weaker and stabilized after prices fell. At noon, the trading price for January-December was 5 pence and 8125, 0.0625 lower than yesterday's closing price.

New York: Although London rubber prices were slightly weaker, New York prices did not change. The market fluctuated slightly.

Securities

New York: The New York securities market had a mixed atmosphere this morning, but the general trend was slightly upward. Sentiment remained optimistic. The Dow Jones 30 Industrial Average opened at 125.75, up 14 pounds sterling. General Motors stock continued to be firm, oil stocks were weaker, railroad stocks opened slightly lower and then rebounded, and public utility stocks continued to fall slightly. No Definite Report on the Rescue of Jones 47

(Beiping) Regarding the outcome of the negotiations for the rescue of British journalist Jones, as of today, the Chahar Provincial Government has not yet received a report from those responsible for the negotiations. According to sources familiar with the matter, the bandits are holding Jones near the Chahar-Jehol border and moving him around constantly, without a fixed address. It is believed that someone within the bandits is intercepting him, and the areas where the bandits travel are not accessible to our security forces. Currently, Zhang Yunji and others, who are responsible for negotiating with the bandits on behalf of the Chahar Provincial Government, are in contact with the bandits somewhere near Guyuan. However, due to the bandits' treachery and lack of sincerity, continued efforts are still needed. Reports that Jones has escaped are confirmed to be speculation. The British Embassy in Beiping is very concerned about this matter. Yesterday and today, they sent personnel to the Beiping Political Affairs Reorganization Committee Military Branch and the Japanese Embassy Military Attaché's Office to discuss all aspects. Japanese Military Attaché Takahashi has telegraphed Chengde to inquire whether there are bandits holding Jones in Jehol, hoping to rescue him locally, but has not yet received a reply from Chengde. (Special dispatch, 8th)

(Beiping) Authorities are finding it extremely difficult to handle the Jones kidnapping case. The kidnappers appear to have handed Jones over to another group of bandits. It is reported that the new bandits are demanding a ransom of 100,000 yuan. Jones has probably been taken to the Chahar-Jehol border, but the exact location is difficult to ascertain, as the kidnappers are constantly moving. The authorities are currently doing everything possible to contact the new bandits. (Reuters dispatch, 8th)

Bandits in Wen'an and Ba County Have Been Defeated 48

(Tianjin) Shang Zhen stated that the bandits in the reed marshes of Wen'an and Ba County have been defeated. Currently, the areas with the highest bandit activity in the province are Wen'an, Ba County, Renqiu in the north, and Daming, Feixiang, Quzhou, and Xingtai in the south. It was previously planned to organize three guerrilla detachments to search the three areas, which will be implemented soon. First, the troops will suppress the bandits, and then heavy troops will be stationed in the areas with the most bandits. Knowledgeable county magistrates will be appointed, and both military and political measures will be taken to fundamentally achieve the effect of suppression. Although there have been bandit disturbances in the war zone, and they have even occupied Taipingzhai in Qian'an, they have been repelled by Zhang Yantian's troops. It is expected that they will not be rampant. The troops of Zhang Qingyu and Zhang Yantian are sufficient to handle the situation. (Special dispatch, 8th)

(Beiping) The bandits disturbing the area between Shanhaiguan and Shihe have been severely attacked by Zhang Yantian's troops. The bandits were driven from Luanhekou, Chengziyu, and Jiumenkou. Due to the relentless pursuit of the security forces, they fled out of Yiyuan Pass on the night of the 7th. The security forces are pursuing them on the 8th. (Special dispatch, 8th)

(Beiping) Liu Guitang's troops, numbering over 1,500, have crossed the Great Wall line into Tangjiakou and Luowenyu, and have reached the northern border of Zunhua. There are also reports that they have entered Malanyu. On the 6th, the county government convened an important meeting of the police and militia, deciding to dispatch a large militia force to the border of the second district to intercept them. (Special dispatch, 8th)

(Beiping) The bandits in the reed marshes of Wen'an and Ba County infiltrated the border area between Renqiu and Xiong County on the 7th. A regiment from the 32nd Army was dispatched to block them. The militias of nearby counties have also been mobilized to assist in the suppression. (Special dispatch, 8th)

(Beiping) There are many reed marshes in Wen'an, Ba County, and other places. Recently, a group of 700 to 800 bandits have been hiding in them. After being surrounded and suppressed by Shang Yi's troops, a part of them, numbering 200 to 300, infiltrated Panggezhuang and other areas in Wanping County yesterday morning. It is now reported that these bandits have fled towards the war zone after being suppressed by local militia troops. (Special dispatch, 8th)

Western Shandong Disaster Area: Over 300 Li Wide; Representatives from Ten Counties Gather in Jining to Discuss Relief; Wang Shaochang Hopes Central Government Will Effectively Block the Breach 87

Jinan correspondence, according to a long-distance telephone call from Jining, since the Yellow River breached in Juancheng, the flood has been rushing southeast. For three weeks, the flood has been spreading, and half of western Shandong has been submerged. The disaster area covers more than ten counties, with a width of over 300 li from east to west and a length of 250 li from north to south, a vast expanse of water. Moreover, the breaches are not blocked, and the water source is abundant, continuing to spread. It is unknown where it will end. Millions of disaster victims are gathering in Jining every day, no less than 20,000 to 30,000 people. Representatives from ten counties, including Zhengcheng, Zhangcheng, Juye, Jiaxiang, Heze, Jining, Dongping, Wenshang, Jinxiang, and Yutai, gathered in Jining to discuss the Yellow River disaster relief issue. Wang Shaochang, director of the Shandong County Administration Construction Experimental Zone, believes that if the breaches are not blocked for one day, the Yellow River disaster will not be reduced for one day. He took the opportunity of Shandong Construction Director Zhang Honglie attending the Yellow River prevention and control meeting in Beijing to send a telegram to Zhang, asking him to describe the disaster situation in western Shandong in detail in Beijing, in order to urge the central government to pay close attention and take effective measures to block the breaches. He also hoped that the central government would send an envoy to console the 4.5 million starving disaster victims. The wording was earnest, with every word a tear. The original text is recorded below.

To Brother Zhang Youshan, Shandong Construction Director, Nanjing Central Hotel: Yesterday, after shaking hands in farewell, I immediately sent the proposed measures to universally rescue the disaster victims. This morning, the county magistrates and representatives of the heavily affected counties, totaling ten counties including Juancheng, Yuncheng, Juye, Jiaxiang, Heze, Jining, Dongping, Wenshang, Jinxiang, and Yutai, gathered at this office to discuss the Yellow River disaster issue. Feeling that the submersion and blocking of the breaches are not imminent, I humbly believe that you are responsible for the construction of the entire province and are currently responsible for controlling the Yellow River. I dare to inform you of the severity of the disaster in the ten counties under the jurisdiction of this district office, and its impact on the overall national situation and national consciousness. I hope that the leading figures of the central government and the Party, as well as the people of Qilu who are staying in Beijing, will investigate. Since July 10, when the Yellow River breached at Dongzhuang, Juancheng, with four breaches, it has been flowing eastward, vast and boundless, taking seven-tenths of the entire river's flow. In less than ten days, northern Heze and southern Juancheng have become wetlands. It spread eastward to Yuncheng, Juye, and Jiaxiang, covering 300 li from east to west and 80 to 250 li from north to south. The county towns of the three counties only remain in the middle of the vast flood. The Yellow River reached Wang Laohu Village and divided into three streams. One stream headed towards Dongping and Wenshang, irrigating West Lake in Dongping. One stream headed north of Jining City, irrigating Nanwang Lake, endangering Jining County. One stream headed between Jining and Jinxiang, overflowing the Zhao Wang River and entering the Nanyang, Dushan, and Zhaoyang Lakes, blocked by the North Jiangsu dam, turned north and stagnated. The Nanyang Lake dam in southern Yutai collapsed in August. The Yellow River rushed like thunder, directly hitting Yutai County. The county magistrate was so angry that he wanted to die and almost sacrificed himself. This stream has the potential to seep westward from Shan County and enter the old Yellow River course in southern Henan and northern Jiangsu. Moreover, Heze Zhengcheng frequently reported that the second breach was expanding northward, and the fifth and sixth breaches were as wide as 500 zhang. At this time of summer and autumn with heavy rainfall, there is no hope of closure. The number of disaster victims in the ten counties is 4.5 million. The disaster area covers over 300 li from east to west and 250 li from north to south, completely submerged. In the face of such an unprecedented catastrophe, I have not heard of any overall relief efforts, but only seen neighboring provinces building dams. Among these 4.5 million people, the number of people gradually gathering at the Jining Station to wait for relief every day is no less than 20,000. The provincial government sent five trains to transport them to various counties, but it was still insufficient. However, this is limited to the old and weak. The able-bodied men crouching on the roofs and treetops, and the hundreds of thousands of people struggling on the embankments, are burning with hunger, soaked in rain, and resentful. They have gone from disappointment to resentment towards the state and local officials. These hundreds of thousands of resentful people may not choose the advantages and disadvantages and take risks. This is something that Shaochang dares not expect. The smoke and Yellow River water are deepening the harm to the people of Lu. The people of Lu are not worthy of pity, but if the breaches are not blocked, the water will continue to flow eastward, increasing without decreasing. Even if it does not seize the canal and enter the Huai, the lack of water in Jining has already approached the Tianjin-Pukou Railway line, and the Hanzhuang Station is gradually being affected. The water overflowing from the Yutai Lake bank is flowing southwest, disrupting the Longhai Railway line from Jinxiang, Shan, and Cao. It is a matter of days. Shaochang cares about the overall situation, grieves for his hometown, and dares not fail to report what he feels is dangerous. I am willing to take advantage of my trip to Beijing to relay the situation on your behalf. If it can urge the central government to pay close attention and take effective measures to block the breaches, and send an envoy to console these 4.5 million people, then I will accept the grace gratefully. Not only will the people of this part of Shandong be fortunate, but the revival of the entire nation's consciousness in the Yellow River and Huai River basins and the national transportation will depend on it. I am telegraphing urgently and feel extremely apprehensive. Brother Wang Shaochang bows with respect.

Guangdong Province: Three Rivers Experience Another Flash Flood; Low-Lying Areas Along the Rivers Inundated; Vast Expanse of Water Along the Guangzhou-Kowloon and Guangdong-Hankou Railways 88

Guangzhou Correspondence, the East, West, and North Rivers in Guangdong Province had just receded in mid-July, but unexpectedly at the end of the month, there were more than ten days of continuous heavy rain in various places, and flash floods broke out in the river basins. The river water gradually rose. It was found that in the upper reaches of the East River, torrential rain started on July 30 and lasted for three days and nights. By the 3rd of this month, the water level had risen by more than five feet again, a total increase of more than eleven feet. The average water depth in Heyuan, Wuhua, Longchuan, Laolong, and Huizhou and Guanyinge in the upper reaches was over a zhang, and all the fields along the river were inundated. The water depth in various villages outside the southeast gate of Heyuan County was five to six feet, and all places in Da Yuanling and Luocun were flooded. Low-lying areas in Taiping Middle Road, Bajiao River Estuary, and Niugang Street in the city were also flooded to the knees. Hengli, Qingzhou, and Nanmen Townships, Xiangyi Market, Yangshan New Market, Qinglongtan, Baini Pond, and Xiami Street, Xihu Huanhu, and Luxiushui Lake in Huiyang County became giant pools. Residents moved furniture by boat in a state of chaos. Su Village, Xiana, and Ma Si in Boluo County also became wetlands. Rice fields near Shilong in Dongguan can also be traversed by boat. The mature rice waves seen along the Guangzhou-Kowloon Railway have now turned into a scene of water and sky, and the losses to agricultural production are significant. All main and county roads in the eastern district were blocked by water and could not be used. The upper reaches of the North River have been discharging flash floods for days, and the Zhen River in Shaozhou has failed to act as a flood discharge outlet, so the flood spread to Qujiang, Yingde, and Qingyuan counties. Several sections of the south section of the Guangdong-Hankou Railway had their tracks washed away and were temporarily closed to traffic. The floodwater near the villages along the Guangdong Railway was as high as thirty feet, and the shallowest places were also about two zhang. The upper section of Shaozhou Road was only repaired on the 2nd, and normal traffic resumed on the 3rd. However, the bus route on the Yingde branch line has not yet resumed. Most of the shops in Yingde Town were flooded to the second floor, and people traveled by boat, which greatly affected business. The number of fields and huts that were flooded is countless. Yesterday, Yingde County Magistrate Tan Yuanchao telegraphed to report the disaster as follows: "The flood in the county has risen to more than two zhang, and the trend is still continuing. The county seat and the villages along the river have become wetlands. Six percent of the early rice has been submerged, and all the late rice seedlings have been flooded. The number of people drowned will be reported in detail. Please allocate funds to provide relief to the disaster victims. Yingde County Magistrate Tan Yuanchao bows." Also, the Yingde County Party Department telegraphed on the 2nd, saying, "The flash flood has risen to more than two zhang. Ripe rice, new seedlings, houses, and livestock have been almost completely submerged. Wails of sorrow can be heard everywhere, and people are waiting to be fed." Also, the northern flood at 2:00 PM has poured into the villages of Qingyuan and Hu Jiang, which bear the brunt of the disaster. At 10:00 PM on the 2nd, the water outside the Qingyuan County seat reached the knees, and most of the shops inside and outside the city closed to avoid the flood. The Sanjiaoji and Huatang dikes on the opposite bank of the county seat were washed away by the water, and fields and houses were submerged. In addition, the Binjiang area and the Buhui area were all flooded, and vegetables and grains were completely lost. The Qingyuan to Yinzhangou road and the Qingyuan to Yangshan road had their roadbeds destroyed by the water, and buses were temporarily suspended, making transportation extremely inconvenient. On the West River side, which was the most severely affected by the previous flood, the accumulated water had just receded when flash floods arrived again. Zhaoqing City was also hit by a hurricane on the evening of the 20th of last month, and most of the overhead power lines were destroyed. The number of small boats with broken masts and sails was also large. Near Foshan in Nanhai County, rainwater flooded all 28 villages in Funanbao and 21 villages in Xilongbao in the Ninth District, and the fields were submerged in water. The streets of Foshan Town were also two feet deep in water, and transportation in nearby villages was by boat. At present, the water in the upper reaches of the West River is still rushing in. The water level in Foshan has risen by more than two zhang from July 26 to the 2nd of this month. If it rains again, it will be easy to repeat the disaster of the previous time. (August 4)

A Thousand-Li Colt Arrives in Jinan: Abdominal Hair Resembles Scales, Called a Dragon Seed; Can Travel 60 Li Per Hour 89

Jinan correspondence, in Shijiazhuang, northeast of Gaotang County, northern Shandong, a farmer named Liu Zhizu (courtesy name Changle) has a black mule. In the spring of the year before last, it suddenly gave birth to a colt with a strange shape and a sensitive and intelligent nature, able to understand human language and run extremely fast. People call it a thousand-li colt. Liu also treasures it like a precious jewel. This spring, upon hearing people say that Wang Yilan in Tianjin (who had studied in the United States) was good at training livestock, such as mules, horses, dogs, and sheep, and could teach them various skills, Liu transported it to Tianjin, which was reported in newspapers at the time. Recently, Liu Jiesan, the nephew of Liu Zhizu, came to Jinan and told Shandong Provincial Chairman Han Fuju that he intended to sell the colt, but because this rare animal was produced in Shandong, it should be preserved in Shandong Province. Han agreed with this, so he sent Adjutant Guan Shilian to Tianjin to negotiate with Liu Zhizu, and then transported the mule and colt to Jinan yesterday (the 6th). Liu and his nephew also came. Liu and others arrived in Jinan at 4:30 PM. Upon hearing the news, people at the station rushed to see it, and the crowd was so large that it was difficult to move. Then Liu led it to the provincial government. From the station, through Er Ma Road, Puhe Gate, Guhuashi Street, and West Main Street, the viewers along the way were like a wall. Some even came from outside the city to see it. The police, fearing that the crowd would cause chaos, tried their best to maintain order. In front of the provincial government's auditorium, Advisor Han Guansan first tried to ride it, and it was indeed very brave and different from ordinary animals. Chairman Han also visited it in front of his office. The owner then ordered the colt to perform various skills, first calling its name, then making it perform handshakes (raising its hooves very high to shake hands), bowing, asking for peace, picking up objects with its mouth, turning forward, turning backward, turning left and right halfway, various turning methods, various walking methods, and walking four characters, walking sideways, running, riding to find objects, and other skills, more than forty kinds in total. As for the walking speed, according to Liu Zhizu, it travels one li per minute, but during the trial last year, it only walked a few li before it started to sweat, so it was not allowed to continue walking. Based on this calculation, it should be able to travel 60 li per hour. The unique points of this colt are many. Its body is gray-red, with long hairs like silver needles. Its legs are thin, its hooves are small, there is a blessing and longevity hair whorl in the middle of its head, there are longevity hair whorls inside and outside the tips of both ears, there is a birth collar hair under its mouth, the hair under its neck grows against the grain, forming a triangle in front, there are eyes in the inner legs, and it always accumulates round or oval-shaped tears. This colt's tears are crescent-shaped, there are short hairs on the bottom of its hooves, and the white pearl hair on its belly resembles scales. From its head to its tail, it is a mane, about an inch high, and its tail is neither donkey-like nor horse-like, resembling bamboo joints.

Chairman Han then returned to his office and called Liu Zhizu and Liu Jiesan in. He first asked about the origin of the colt. According to them, the mother of the colt (a black mule) had been unable to conceive when mated with horses or donkeys in the past. The year before last, it was not mated, but suddenly conceived, and this colt was born on February 2nd. It is said to be a dragon seed, and no one saw it. When this colt was first born, it had a unique shape and was extremely sensitive. It ate more feed and less grass. Now, its milk teeth have fallen out, and it only has two teeth. After this, the mother mule has not been able to conceive. Chairman Han then said, "I first heard people say that this colt was produced in Gaotang, and then I saw it reported in the newspapers. Because I did not plan to buy it, I did not pay attention to it. Otherwise, I would have asked Gaotang County to send it to me to see it earlier. A few days ago, my nephew reported it to me, so I asked them to transport it here for me to see. If you want to sell it, I will keep it, because it is produced in Shandong and should be preserved in Shandong. In fact, I personally do not need this thing." Liu repeatedly said that he was willing to dedicate it to the Chairman. Han said, "If you say you want to give it to me, I will definitely not accept it, because the government will never take a single blade of grass or a piece of wood from the people for free." Finally, Liu Jie said that he had spent more than a thousand yuan on feeding and transporting it to Tianjin over the years. Chairman Han then ordered that a thousand yuan be given to them, and the colt was kept temporarily in the horse stable and one person was left to feed it. The black mule was ordered to be taken back. Liu thanked him and left.

Flood Situation in the Upper Reaches of Anhui Province: Inspection of River Embankment Flood Control; The Situation in the Upper Reaches is More Important Than in the Lower Reaches; Provincial Government Sends Letter to Water Conservancy Agencies Reporting 90

Anqing dispatch: This year's river water is rising sharply. The water levels in various places within Anhui Province are almost the same as the highest water levels in the twentieth year of the Republic. The area around Susong County in the upper reaches is even level with the highest water level of the twentieth year. Judging from past experience, the situation of dikes and embankments in Anhui Province is more important in the upper reaches than in the lower reaches, and the left bank of the upper reaches is more important than the right bank. This is because the area has rivers outside and lakes inside, forming a strip of land, with only a special line of earthen dikes acting as a barrier for hundreds of miles. Also, a part of it reaches the intersection of Hubei, Jiangxi, and Anhui provinces, with long dikes and complicated jurisdictions, making comprehensive prevention difficult. Liu Bohua, Chairman of the Provincial Government, recently took the reported materials, inspected the situation, and sent a letter to the Yangtze River Water Resources Commission and the National Economic Council. The main points of the letter are as follows: (1) Yangjia on the opposite bank of Anqing is the northwest acute angle of Dongliu Guangfeng Embankment, located at the turning point of the river flow, and the terrain is very important. Fortunately, most of the section is sandy, but the embankment body is still thick, so there is no danger. (2) The Dongliu City Protection Embankment is connected to the main embankment and protects the city defense, which is of great importance to the military. After landing and inspecting, the embankment surface is only about two feet away from the water. The west embankment is particularly dangerous. Local gentry should be summoned to mobilize everyone to cooperate in rescue. At the same time, the county magistrate Zhang Zexie should be ordered to increase manpower day and night to raise and thicken the embankment. (3) The line of river embankment from Wangjiang Huayang to Huaining Lao Lake is winding like a belt. Each dike attached to the embankment considers the river embankment outside and prevents mountain floods and lake waves inside, making the work very difficult. At that time, leakage occurred in the Dongxing Embankment, and the Baoxing Embankment was also in danger. The Construction Department had previously issued sacks and cash to urge Wangjiang County to do its best to rescue. Zhen Hua also sent Commissioner Ni Wenzheng with 500 yuan to assist County Magistrate Hong in strengthening prevention and rescue. (4) The four major dikes in Susong County—Tongren, Dingkou, Jingjiang, and Mahua—have been strictly supervised and repaired last year to meet the specified dike standards. The dike surfaces in all places are four or five feet higher than the current water surface, and the inner river and lake dikes are also two or three feet higher than the water surface. However, the soil quality in several places contains sand, which is most prone to leakage. Fortunately, the county magistrate is very diligent in inspections, and the dike-protecting laborers also know how to work hard. The Construction Department has also taught various flood control and rescue methods and distributed materials for preparation, so there should be no danger. (5) The Mahua Embankment is a large dike of common interest to Hubei, Jiangxi, and Anhui provinces. It has always been repaired by the three provinces according to a percentage share. Last year's repairs were also done separately. This time, the dike breached in Pengze Yujiapu in Jiangxi Province. It was reported that Director Liu of the Construction Department is setting up rescue efforts there. Zhen Hua and others landed at Yujiapu and walked about five li downwards to inspect the breach. The place is located at No. 15 Bao, District 2 of Pengze County, Jiangxi Province, opposite Shima. After inquiring, the breach occurred at 6:00 PM on July 5th. The outer beach collapsed first, followed by the river embankment. Now the river flow is turbulent, scouring and collapsing over a hundred zhang. According to the original dike surface, it was one zhang and five chi wide and six shi chi higher than the current water surface. In theory, it should not have collapsed. It must be that the new dike had not yet settled, and the stone feet of Madang Mountain on the opposite side were pressing, causing rapid currents to discharge and lead to seepage. The area is sparsely populated, and it was not detected beforehand, so it was difficult to recover from the breach. Now the river flow is overflowing. If it is not blocked and built up quickly, it will endanger the inner dike and harm eight counties in Hubei, Jiangxi, and Anhui provinces. It has been decided by the Chairman of your Commission, the Secretary-General of the National Economic Council Qin, and the Chief Engineer of the Jiangxi Water Conservancy Bureau Qiu to draw up four draft plans for blocking the breach. The Jiangxi Water Conservancy Bureau will first handle the package head work. In addition to sending personnel from the Engineering Department and members for purchasing and transporting materials, our province will also order Susong and Wang counties to send laborers to assist in the work. In addition, the entire river embankment is still intact (note that dikes that collapse during violent floods are not included). If there is no more violent rise, the strength of the dikes can still be barely supported. In addition to continuing to supervise the responsible departments and all county officials and people to step up protection, I have inspected the dike situation in the upper reaches of Anhui Province and hereby inform you for your reference, and request that you follow the four agreed principles for the blocking of the Mahua Embankment, immediately send engineering personnel to guide, and transfer to the National Economic Council to allocate the required construction funds. (August 6th)

Songjiang: Revision of Household Registration Change Reporting

Our province is implementing the Baojia system. All counties in the province have completed the three-level organization. The township Baojia chiefs have all been legally produced. They should take over the investigation and reporting of household registration changes. According to the original method, the Jia chiefs verbally reported to the Bao chiefs, who reported to the township office and then to the district office. After compiling the statistics, they were submitted to the county for record. Only in this way can the accuracy of the household registration be ensured. According to the law, household registration changes are divided into eight categories: relocation, birth, death, marriage, inheritance, separation, employment, and disappearance. Now the provincial order has been revised to four items, roughly divided into increases and decreases in households and increases and decreases in population. It is reported that all districts will be notified to comply.

Kunshan: Farmers in Beicun Robbed by Bandits

At the home of farmer Ma Jinsheng in Beicun, about two li from Zhangpu Town, at about 1:00 AM the other night, six or seven bandits suddenly broke through the wall, speaking in local dialect and holding weapons. The Ma family members were all asleep. When they jumped up, they were confined to a room by the bandits, who scared them into silence. Then they entered the room to search and rob. Neighbors heard the noise and sounded the gong to warn. The bandits fled with their loot. By the time the villagers came to arrest them, the bandits had gone far away. Upon checking, the lost items totaled more than 300 yuan in silver and banknotes. Yesterday morning, Ma came to the city to report to the county government to investigate and arrest the fleeing bandits.

Suzhou: Suzhou City Plans to Open Public Buses

The transportation industry in Suzhou is progressing daily. The Sujia Highway has long been open to traffic. The Suchang, Sukun, and Sumu highways will also be open to traffic one after another in the coming days. The main roads inside and outside the city have been completed by sixty to seventy percent. The opening of Xiangmen and the reconstruction of Banmen are expected to be completed within the year, and the road can also circulate around the city. The Jiangsu Provincial Highway Department is planning to operate public buses inside and outside Suzhou City in the spring of next year. The Wuxian Construction Bureau is currently planning everything. However, the rickshaw drivers' association believes that the operation of public buses inside and outside the city has a great impact on the rickshaw business. Moreover, the Construction Bureau added 500 rickshaw licenses two years ago. At that time, the association raised 80,000 yuan to purchase the licenses and signed a contract stipulating that public buses should not be operated inside and outside the city within three years. Therefore, they plan to ask the Construction Department to postpone the operation of public buses. However, the authorities believe that this contract has expired and is invalid, so it is unlikely to achieve their goal.

Prosecution of Police Officers for Conspiring to Murder for Money

The case of Gu Agen, a devotee of the Zhou family nunnery in Guan Zai Nong, who was killed, has caused a sensation in society. Whether it was suicide or murder is unclear. The court believes it was murder and that the police chief of the jurisdiction is a major suspect. The Public Security Bureau believes it was suicide. The Public Security Bureau has transferred and detained the suspects, Inspector Hong Shiqin and Patrol Chief Xu Baosheng, to the court for interrogation. The prosecutor has concluded the investigation and prosecuted Inspector Hong Shiqin and Patrol Chief Xu Baosheng for inciting murder, intimidating and defrauding property, and forging documents and dereliction of duty; Police Officer He Naikang for murder and forgery; Police Officer Yang Shunfu for intimidation and dereliction of duty; and Tie Xie Qianshugang for forgery. The criminal court will publicly try the case immediately. It is also reported that Yan Lian, the director of the First Public Security Bureau in charge, has resigned due to negligence. The major suspicious case has now come to light. As for Hong Shiqin's motive for killing Gu, it was because Wang Weinong, who had absconded with money, was hiding there. It was rumored that there were thirty jin of banknotes hidden there, so he started to plot for money. Wang will now be escorted to the Shanghai court for questioning.

Wuxi: Strict Prohibition of Electric Hair Perming

The Municipal Public Security Bureau held a police affairs meeting yesterday. Chairman Chen Yuchu decided: (1) The police officers who graduated from the Police Training School are still assigned to the third-level police service. Some of them apply for resignation for no reason or deliberately neglect their duties in order to be dismissed, which goes against the original purpose of the training. Strict restrictions should be imposed, and the graduation certificates should be recovered. (2) Ms. Gu from Dongmen died from injuries sustained from an electric hair perm. Hair perms are against the principles of the new life of simplicity and frugality, and electric perms cause significant losses in terms of economy and time. Now that there has been a death from electric perming, it should be strictly prohibited. There are three or four businesses in the city that use electric hair perming, such as Dahua. It has been decided to order them to be investigated and prohibited to prevent life-threatening risks and maintain the new life movement.

Reporters' Association Elects Petition Representatives

The Municipal Journalists' Association held a temporary members' meeting yesterday afternoon. Chairman Sun Dexian decided: (1) Sun Xiangfeng, Wu Guanchong, Hua Jinji, and Sun Dexian were elected as representatives to petition in Beijing to amend the Publication Law, and Jiang Zhongliang, Su Xingwu, Shi Qinglin, Zhou Hanquan, Wang Xiehui, and Fan Liqi were elected to receive colleagues from other counties who came to Wuxi to gather. (2) Chen Hongjun and others proposed that an article in the Shanghai Journalism Quarterly defamed and slandered the entire journalism community in Wuxi by publishing the history and current situation of the news industry in various places. It was decided to appoint Jiang Zhongliang and Chen Hongjun to handle the litigation.

Haimen: Adultery Leads to Murder

Zhang, the wife of Zhu Shaodong, a villager in Le, District Six (i.e., Zhang), is in her thirties. She is quite promiscuous and restless. She had an affair with her neighbor Ni Zhaozhen two years ago, and they were in close contact. Recently, she became acquainted with a young neighbor, Liu Guomin. Ni found out about the affair and was extremely angry. On the afternoon of the fifth, he took advantage of Liu and Zhang's secret rendezvous to gather Ni Shisheng, Ni Shaoying, Fan Longgou, Li Wenxiu, and Zhang Xuewen to catch the adulterers. Liu was awakened from his sleep and tried to break through to escape, but he accidentally fell into the river and drowned. More than ten soldiers from the Third Security Brigade stationed in Fu'an Town were patrolling and learned the truth. They arrested Ni Zhaozhen, Ni Shisheng, Ni Shaoying, Fan Longgou, Li Wenxiu, Zhang Xuewen, Zhu Shaodong, and Zhu Zhang and took them to the brigade headquarters. Yesterday afternoon, they were sent to the county government for interrogation. Chen, the adjudicator, went to Qian yesterday morning to conduct the investigation.

Nantong: Using the Baojia System to Investigate and Suppress Opium and Drugs

The six counties of Tong, Ru, Chong, Hai, Jing, and Qi decided to use the Baojia system to investigate and suppress opium and drugs after a meeting on drug investigation and suppression. It was stipulated that the Baojia chiefs should report all private opium smokers, drug users, and suspected traffickers and manufacturers in their respective Baojia within one month, with a pledge of joint liability, and report to the county government for search. Baojia chiefs who know the situation but do not report will be punished according to the severity of the circumstances.

Verdict in the Case of Hiding a Lover in a Cellar

Zhai Hede from Jinsha had an incestuous relationship with his niece Xiao. Unable to elope together, he dug a cellar at home, set up beds, tables, and stools inside, and covered it with a reed shed to hide his niece. The girl's father discovered it and filed a lawsuit with the court. The criminal court sentenced Qu Hede to months in prison for enticing the girl.

Letter to the Editor 91

Dear Editor, I was shocked to read the news "The Danbao Newspaper Office was Destroyed..." in your newspaper's Kunshan dispatch on the 7th of this month. After investigation, the Kunshan Daily was established by the shareholders who elected Lu Jiandan, Jin Chenglu, and Chen Fengge to jointly apply for registration. All the necessary items used by the Daily Newspaper Office were borrowed from the Chenbao Newspaper Office by Cheng Liu, with Chen Fengge, Zou De, Xu Liangqiu as guarantors (with IOUs to prove). Now, due to illegal acts by internal personnel, Cheng Liu and Fengge exercised their powers and decided to temporarily suspend publication from August 3rd in order to thoroughly rectify the situation. On the afternoon of the 4th, they went to the office to return all the necessary items borrowed from the Chenbao Newspaper Office in order to complete the procedures. The destruction reported in your newspaper is completely untrue. Fearing that the outside world does not know the truth, we hereby clarify the facts and hope that you will correct the letter accordingly. Jin Chenglu, Chen Fengge, Zou Xiaotan, jointly. August 7th.
