Local News

Fundraising for Provincial Flood Relief Association: Inaugural Meeting Held Yesterday; Declaration for Donations Passed, Organizational Regulations Approved; Request Made to City Government to Advise Unification of Disaster Relief Organizations 92

Shanghai society, recognizing the severity of this year's floods, initiated the establishment of the Shanghai Fundraising Association for Provincial Flood Relief. The inaugural meeting was held yesterday (the 8th) at 4:00 PM at the Renji Hall on Yunnan Road. Over a hundred leaders from various sectors of the city attended. Mayor Wu presided over the meeting, which promptly approved the association's personnel, organizational regulations, and a declaration. Several important resolutions regarding fundraising for flood relief were also discussed. Details are as follows:

Attendees: Leaders from Various Sectors

The leaders from various sectors who attended yesterday's inaugural meeting included Wu Tiecheng, Xu Shiying, Song Ziliang, Huang Renzhi, Lu Wen'an, Wang Peiyuan, Shu Chushi, Du Ruisheng, Wang Xiaolai, Chen Timin, Monk Chidian, Peng Yuncen, Tang Renxin, Chen Liangyu, Shi Weidu, Wen Lanting, Shen Tianxin, Gu Xinyi, Li Dachao, Lu Bohong, Huang Bodu, Qu Wenliu, Li Zizai, Zhao Yiwu, Li Wuyun, Baker, Quan Shaowu, Chen Jicheng, Cheng Jingsheng, Pan Xulun, Zhao Duanyuan, Zhu Xiecheng, Yin Guanzhi, Chen Binhe, Han Juemin, Wang Yiting, Wu Yunzhai, Chen Lengseng, Yu Zuoting, Qian Zhonghua, Chu Huiseng, Pan Zhe, Sun Choucheng, Wang Dizhai, Jiang Qingfan, Qian Xinzhi, and others, totaling over a hundred people.

Wu Tiecheng Elected Temporary Chairman

The meeting commenced at 4:00 PM, with attendees electing Mayor Wu as chairman. After customary formalities, Chairman Wu delivered a report, stating that since the beginning of summer this year, the Yangtze and Yellow River basins have experienced successive floods, severely impacting the lives and property of people on both banks. Chairman Xu personally traveled to the disaster areas, braving the heat to conduct detailed inspections, a spirit that is deeply admirable. Our country has suffered from disasters almost every year in recent years, leading to extreme social and economic decline. Shanghai, since the January 28th Incident, has seen sluggish industrial and commercial activity, but it is still fortunate compared to the inland areas. However, Shanghai's prosperity depends on the recovery of the inland economy. I often say that Shanghai is like a fish, and the inland is like water. A fish without water cannot survive. Therefore, if we want to restore Shanghai's prosperity, we must rely on alleviating the distress of the inland areas. Since the lives of Shanghai people are better than those of the inland people, we should still do our best to fulfill our obligation of mutual assistance in the same boat. This year's flood is more severe than the flood of 1931. This year, Shanghai's economic situation is worse than in 1931, so we should work harder to ensure that this year's results are better than in previous years.

Xu Shiying Reports on the Disaster Situation

Following this, Xu Shiying reported, stating that since mid-June of this year, continuous torrential rains have fallen in the provinces along the Yangtze River, causing flash floods. Provinces such as Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi, and Anhui have experienced either prolonged waterlogging or the collapse of dikes, inundating fields and washing away people and livestock. The disaster situation is extremely dire. I personally inspected the disaster areas and witnessed the tragic conditions. According to reports, the number of affected counties is as follows: Hubei has 51 counties and cities, Hunan has 37 counties, including 15 severely affected counties, Jiangxi has 48 counties, including 13 severely affected counties, and Anhui has 13 counties. The number of disaster victims is 7.15 million in Hubei, 4.1 million in Hunan, and over 300,000 in Anhui, bringing the total, including Jiangxi, to over 14 million people. The affected area, including severely and lightly affected areas, is estimated to reach 100,000 square kilometers. The extent of farmland inundation can be inferred from this. The number of people drowned is also over 100,000. The total direct and indirect public and private losses are estimated to be no less than 500 million yuan. Moreover, the flood-stricken areas, such as Tianmen, Hanchuan, Jianli, Shishou, and Gong'an counties in Hubei, and Changde and Nanxian counties in Hunan, are known for their rich agricultural production. This devastating flood has wiped out their vitality, and relief is urgently needed. Now, the Yellow River basin, including Shandong, Hebei, and Henan, has also reported disasters, with damage comparable to that of Hunan and Jiangxi provinces. I will continue to inspect those areas. Various sectors of this city have initiated the establishment of the Fundraising Association for Provincial Flood Relief, which is established today. We hope to raise funds as soon as possible to provide relief to the disaster victims. Xu also reported that before the establishment of this association, various parties had already generously donated large sums of money to Renji Hall for relief purposes. These donations will be handed over to this association for disaster relief. Mr. Wang Yiting has already raised 14,534.45 yuan from various parties. Compatriots from Singapore donated 20,000 yuan. The Jincheng Cinema in this city will donate all ticket revenue from today (yesterday) to this association for disaster relief. After Xu's report, Biao Fucheng stood up and proposed that in the future, for overseas compatriots, Mr. Zhu Ziqiao be invited to go to Southeast Asia to conduct fundraising. The chairman indicated acceptance.

Standing in Mourning for Compatriots Who Perished

At this time, Huang Renzhi stood up and stated that listening to Chairman Xu's report on the tragic situation in the disaster areas was unsettling. It is not difficult for us to imagine that the compatriots in the disaster areas are suffering greatly. We are fortunate to be able to live here peacefully. We should do our best to find ways to provide relief to our disaster-stricken compatriots. I request that everyone present stand up and observe three minutes of silence, both to mourn the compatriots who perished and to think of a proper relief plan for the compatriots in distress. The entire assembly unanimously agreed and stood in silence for three minutes.

Declaration of Inaugural Meeting Passed

The declaration of the inaugural meeting was then discussed and the following original text was passed: Since the beginning of summer this year, continuous torrential rains have fallen, causing flash floods. The Yangtze, Huai, Yellow, and Han rivers have all reported disasters successively, with urgent requests for relief pouring in. The situation is extremely dire. The affected areas in Hubei, Hunan, Jiangxi, and Anhui provinces cover more than 150 counties, with over 100,000 people drowned and over 14 million disaster victims awaiting relief. Public and private losses are estimated to be no less than 500 million yuan. Moreover, the expansion of the disaster situation in Shandong, Henan, and Hebei provinces is not yet included. The severity of the disaster even surpasses the flood of 1931. Are not all those crying out for food our brothers and sisters? Knowing that the social economy is already struggling, we are compelled by conscience to provide relief out of brotherly affection and cannot bear to sit idly by. Therefore, we are initiating charitable relief, hoping to provide assistance. We hope that with everyone's efforts, we can overcome the difficulties and prove that human effort can conquer nature. We urge kind-hearted people from all walks of life at home and abroad to take immediate action and share their feelings of hunger and thirst, promoting the desire for universal salvation and relief. We ask for continuous donations of grain, money, and supplies. This association vows to do its best, be practical and realistic, and strive to live up to expectations, alleviate the disaster, and save lives. We have many intentions but no tears to shed. We offer these sincere words and hope for your understanding.

Organizational Regulations Revised and Passed

After the declaration was passed, the organizational regulations were modified and passed. The full text is as follows: Article 1: This association is named the Shanghai Fundraising Association for Provincial Flood Relief. All those who are enthusiastic about charity and support the purpose of this association are members of this association. Article 2: The members of this association shall elect one president and four vice presidents to preside over the association's affairs, approximately ten directors, and approximately ten supervisors, and shall mutually elect standing directors (50-90) and standing supervisors (15-25), who shall be stationed at the association regularly to handle affairs. Article 3: The meetings of this association are as follows: (1) General meetings are convened once a month; (2) Regular meetings are held every week; (3) Emergency meetings may be convened in the event of urgent matters. The association is presided over by the president, and if the president is absent due to circumstances, the vice president shall preside. Article 4: The association shall have one secretary-general and two deputy secretaries-general, who shall be nominated by the standing directors' meeting and shall handle affairs with the approval of the president and vice president. Article 5: This association shall be divided into the following groups: (A) General Affairs Group, in charge of clerical work, accounting, general affairs, receiving and dispatching, records, reporting, and other non-specified matters; (B) Fundraising Group, in charge of planning and fundraising for relief funds and supplies; (C) Finance Group, in charge of receiving relief funds and supplies, storing, remitting, and purchasing grain and seeds; (D) Planning Group, in charge of planning association activities and relief plans; (E) Investigation and Distribution Group, in charge of investigating distribution and facilities related to agricultural and industrial relief; (F) Propaganda Group, in charge of compiling disaster reports and other propaganda matters; (G) Health Group, in charge of managing medicines, treating diseases, preventing epidemics, and all health matters; (H) Audit Group, in charge of auditing relief funds and supplies and the association's financial income and expenditure; (I) Women's Fundraising Group, in charge of planning and fundraising from women's circles at home and abroad. Article 6: Each of the above groups shall have one director and several deputy directors, who shall be nominated by the standing directors' meeting to handle group affairs. Depending on the complexity of the affairs, several staff members may be appointed to handle the affairs of each group, and clerks may be appointed to specialize in writing. Article 7: The president, vice president, standing directors, supervisors, secretary-general, deputy secretary-general, and directors and deputy directors of each group shall all be volunteers. Staff members and clerks who are deemed necessary to be given subsidies may be determined by the standing directors' meeting. Article 8: These regulations shall come into effect from the date of the establishment of this association.

Nomination of President and Directors of Each Group

After the organizational regulations were passed, the association's personnel were immediately nominated. The list is as follows: President: Kong Xiangxi; Vice Presidents: Xu Shiying, Wang Zhengting, Wang Zhen, Wu Tiecheng; General Affairs Group Director: Qu Yingguang; Deputy Directors: Huang Qinglan, Qian Yingqing, Li Dachao; Typhoon Warning Signal Raised by Customs Yesterday; However, According to Father Gherzi's Prediction, the Wind Will Not Be Strong When It Passes Through This Morning 93

According to the Greater Shanghai Evening News yesterday, the typhoon has not dissipated despite passing over a long stretch of land. According to Father Gherzi of the Xujiahui Observatory, it will pass through the area slightly west of Shanghai tonight (the 8th) or tomorrow morning (the 9th). Therefore, this port will experience occasional showers, but there will be no excessive wind. Approximately when the typhoon passes through, there will be strong northeast and southeast winds. This typhoon came from the ocean, passed through Taiwan, and entered the Fujian coast near Xiamen. It seems to have the characteristic of dissipating over land. Its direction turned north or northeast, and it will apparently pass through the border between Jiangxi and Zhejiang. Now it is believed that because it has traveled a long distance over land, the wind force has weakened significantly. Heavy rain fell frequently in this port in the second half of last night (the 7th), and the weather is still cloudy today (the 8th), with occasional rain. The temperature has been greatly reduced. According to the Xujiahui Observatory, the maximum temperature for the whole day was only 85.5 degrees.

Customs Raised Ball Around 2:00 AM yesterday morning, there was heavy rain in this port, which later stopped and started. At about 3:00 PM, wind and rain hit, and the waves outside Wusongkou were dangerous. The waves also rose in the Huangpu River. The Customs issued a typhoon warning signal at 2:00 PM yesterday afternoon. The Shipping Office raised a black ball on the flagpole of the Customs bell tower so that ships could recognize it.

All Ships Suspended Yesterday evening, all ships that should have departed for the Jianghai were suspended due to the warning. The Ningbo-bound Sanbei's Ningxing, China Merchants' Xin Jiangtian, Yangtze River-bound China Merchants' Jianghua, Taikoo's Datong, Jardine's Xin Pinghe, Beiyang-bound China Merchants' Hairui, Taikoo's Dingsheng, Nanhua-bound Taikoo's Yuezhou, Fuzhou-bound Sanbei's Wanxiang, and Wintai-bound Lian'an's Chuanshan, etc., are all known to have been unable to sail. And the ships that should have arrived yesterday, such as Taikoo's Hong Kong-bound Niuzhuang, Hong Kong-Shantou-bound Haikou, Hong Kong-Fuzhou-bound Sichuan, China Merchants Bureau's Tianjin-Yantai-bound Xin Feng, and Qingdao-bound Anxing, etc., were unable to arrive on schedule due to the typhoon.

Precautions Against High Tides State-run China Merchants Bureau, privately-run Sanbei Shipping Company, Ning Shao Shipping Company, British Taikoo Shipping Company, Jardine Shipping Company, and Japanese Nisshin Company jointly decided yesterday to issue a public notice stating: This is to notify that whether you are a shipper or a consignee, if goods are stored in the above-mentioned shipping companies' own or leased warehouses, we will not be responsible for any damage caused to the goods due to high tides. However, within the possible range, our companies will do our best to protect the goods to avoid damage, but the owner of the goods shall still be responsible for the damage. All expenses incurred by the shipping companies to protect the goods shall also be collected from the owner of the goods when the goods are shipped. This is a special notice, August 8, 1935.

Municipal Government Announcement: 100 Mu of Land to Be Requisitioned at Fenglin Bridge for Construction of Zhongshan Hospital 95

According to China News Agency, the baseball field on Route Pére Robert in the French Concession was donated to our country by the board of directors of the American Rockefeller Foundation to build the large-scale Zhongshan Hospital, which was to be presided over by Yan Fuqing. Later, due to obstacles at the site, it was changed to be built near Fenglin Bridge, where more than 100 mu of private land will be requisitioned. The Municipal Government has already submitted it to the Ministry of Interior and issued an announcement for requisition. The announcement reads: The Municipal Land and Health Bureaus, in a report dated May 23, 1935, stated, The Municipal Land Bureau, based on the report of the National Shanghai Medical College and the Shanghai Medical Affairs Board of Directors, reported: To request the Shanghai Municipal Government to forward to the Ministry of Interior for approval to requisition private land for the construction of the Shanghai Zhongshan Hospital and Shanghai Medical College. Our association is preparing to build the Shanghai Zhongshan Hospital to meet the medical needs of the public and to provide practical training for students of Shanghai Medical College to cultivate medical talents. More than 700,000 yuan of construction funds have already been raised, and the board of directors of the American Rockefeller Foundation has donated 130 mu of land on Route Pére Robert in the special district of this city as the site. Recently, due to obstacles, it was decided by the general meeting to change the location to be built on land near Fenglin Bridge in this city. Fenglin Bridge is located in the south of the city, and the population is prosperous, but there is still a lack of good hospitals and medical facilities. The mayor, concerned about the people's suffering, once advocated setting up a hospital there. This is under your administration, which is inspiring. It is found that the boundaries of the eighth map Chengziwei in the South Shanghai District, (1) No. 4, the entire boundary, east to Fenglin Bridge Road, south to Mulonggang, west to Dongmiao Bridge Road, north to Shenjiabang Road, (2) No. 3, the southwest corner, part of the boundary, east to the land of the Shanghai County Education Bureau, south to Shenjiabang Road, west to Dongmiao Bridge Road, north to French Book No. 423, the entire base, can be used as the construction site for Zhongshan Hospital and Shanghai Medical College. However, among them, there are more than 30 owners, and private acquisition is quite difficult. Shanghai Medical College is a national teaching and academic institution, and Zhongshan Hospital is a charitable public welfare institution, and also a practical hospital for Shanghai Medical College. Therefore, in accordance with Article 1 of the Shanghai Municipality Land Requisition Management Regulations and Article 2, Item 7 of the Land Requisition Law, a detailed plan, together with maps and building plans, are prepared and submitted to request verification and forwarding to the Municipal Government to transfer to the Ministry of Interior to allow the requisition of a base of 100 mu within the site to facilitate the construction of the project. Furthermore, the entire construction project of Zhongshan Hospital was contracted early and cannot be delayed. I hope that a quick review will be truly beneficial to both the public and ethics. The reports, along with the attached maps and other documents, were sent to the bureau, which considered that the case concerned the construction of a hospital and medical college, and the requisition of private land was about 100 mu. A letter was immediately sent from the Health Bureau to conduct a detailed review based on the architectural style and a summary of the plan. It was found that the scope of the land proposed to be acquired by the college and others was indeed necessary in fact, and it was reasonable to report the situation and attach the original plan and maps. We request verification and reply, etc. In accordance with Article 2, Item 7 of the Land Requisition Law, it should be approved. In addition to replying for verification, we also request that you instruct us to handle it in accordance with the law. In accordance with the provisions of Article 9 of the same law, the matters to be announced are listed below, so that the public will know. This is a special announcement, with the following details: (1) Sponsor of the business: National Shanghai Medical College and Shanghai Medical Affairs Board of Directors; (2) Type of business: Educational and academic and charitable undertakings; (3) Area where the business is conducted: Eighth map, Chengziwei, South Shanghai District, (1) The entire boundary of No. 4, east to Fenglin Bridge Road, south to Mulonggang, west to Dongmiao Bridge Road, north to Shenjiabang Road, (2) A part of the southwest corner of No. 3, the boundary east to the land of the Shanghai County Education Bureau, south to Shenjiabang Road, west to Dongmiao Bridge Road, north to French Book No. 423, the entire base. The total land requisitioned for the above two places is 100 mu.

Party and Government Organs Maintain Traffic; Limit Rickshaw Pullers to Resume Work; Rickshaw Pullers Obey Orders but Unwilling to Enter the French Concession 96

The 40,000 rickshaw pullers of the French Concession, dissatisfied with the registration organized by the French Concession, went on strike on the morning of the 6th. After a conflict, because the French Concession authorities had no intention of canceling the registration, the strike continued yesterday. At the same time, the rickshaw pullers, driven by grief and indignation, pried off the French Concession license plates from public concession vehicles traveling in Nanshi, in order to sanction their undermining of solidarity.

Rickshaw Company Petition

Yesterday morning at 9 o'clock, the Rickshaw Guild specially sent representatives Qiu Chunshan, Yu Dajin, Zhang Huaiyang, Zhou Jinyuan, and others, a total of four people, to submit a document to the municipal government in the city center to petition. The Section Chief of the Second Section, Zhang Yiyu, received them. First, they stated the situation of the dispute and the resolutions of the car owners' meeting, requesting negotiation. The municipal government representative promised to ask the mayor for instructions.

Social Affairs Bureau Inquiry

The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau summoned representatives of the Rickshaw Guild for questioning yesterday. The car dealer representatives Yu Dajin, Qiu Chunshan, and Zhang Huaiyang attended. The Director of the Labor Welfare Division of the Third Section, Wang Gang, and the staff member of the Second Section, Chen Zeyi, held talks. In addition to inquiring about the process, the representatives of the Social Affairs Bureau also stipulated two measures approved by the municipal government: (1) The municipal government is responsible for negotiating the incident, and car dealers and rickshaw pullers should wait for the municipal government to handle it properly. (2) The Social Affairs Bureau is ordered to advise the trade association to inform the rickshaw pullers to resume work uniformly from tomorrow (the 9th).

Party and Government Order

The guild received an order from the Municipal Party Department yesterday, which read: "In order to comply with the matter, it is found that the industry has suspended business without prior approval, affecting traffic, which is already very serious. Now it is heard that there are plans to expand the area of the business suspension, which will further hinder public security. It is hereby urgently ordered that the association comply with and quickly find ways to persuade all business firms under its jurisdiction not to expand the dispute any further, and to instruct all rickshaw pullers to comply as necessary. This order is imperative." The Social Affairs Bureau approved the order, saying that the matter regarding the French Concession's cross-border arrest and the conflict with rickshaw pullers and forced registration has been submitted to the municipal government for negotiation. They should wait for approval and first resume business as soon as possible to maintain traffic and avoid affecting the livelihood of rickshaw pullers. This is the approval.

Industry Meeting

The Rickshaw Trade Association held a committee meeting at its meeting place on Puyu East Road at 3 pm yesterday. More than 20 people attended, chaired by Qiu Chunshan. First, he reported on the process of petitioning the municipal government and the Social Affairs Bureau's inquiry. The party and government authorities ordered the resumption of work as soon as possible to maintain traffic. After discussion, everyone said that they would respect the authorities' intentions and immediately order all car owners to inform the rickshaw pullers to resume work uniformly and wait for the authorities to resolve the issue.

Rickshaw Pullers' Meeting

Yesterday at 5 pm, rickshaw pullers held a meeting at Nanmatou, attended by more than 200 people, chaired by Shi Changsheng. First, he reported on the progress of the case and the situation of the car owners being ordered to persuade them to resume work. After discussion: (1) How to proceed with the car owners' announcement of resuming work as soon as possible? It was decided that: (A) uniformly resume work on the morning of the 9th; (B) only allowed to operate in Hubei South, and not allowed to be dragged to the French Concession; (3) the loss of strike time should be requested from the guild to negotiate compensation with the French Concession; (4) the medical expenses of the injured should be borne by the French police; (5) negotiate with the French police to hand over the missing rickshaw puller Xue Er (i.e., Xue Ruji).

Rickshaw Pullers' Statement

Rickshaw puller representative Shi Changsheng expressed his opinion that the French Consul-General's words to Mr. Du were puzzling. Rickshaw pullers did not object to the public concession holding registration. The vehicle license plates were issued by the Public Works Bureau, and the Public Works Bureau had the right to add unified control. The Nanshi small license plates were the license plates and steel seals of the Public Utilities Bureau. The French Concession really had no right to govern them. If it must be held, the vehicles with the public concession license plates should also be registered at the same time to be fair. What if the Public Utilities Bureau also wants to register rickshaw pullers? What should be done? The rickshaw pullers' opinion is that if the Public Utilities Bureau registers rickshaw pullers, they may accept it. If the French Concession registers, at least the vehicles with the public concession license plates should be registered at the same time.

Court Hearing

After rickshaw pullers in Shanghai South and Shanghai West declared a strike on the morning of the 6th due to their opposition to the French Municipal Council's registration, conflicts occurred, and tires were deflated. Several people were arrested by the French police and sent to the Special Second Court for interrogation. In the past two days, some striking rickshaw pullers have been blocking the road and deflating tires. At a little more than 1 pm on the 7th, a detective of the French police arrested Gu Changxing, a 16-year-old boy from Jiangbei Xinghua, on Blue Weiai Road for deflating rickshaw tires. He was sent to the Eighth Criminal Court of the Special Second Court yesterday. At 10 am, Judge Li Changnian interrogated him. Police Attorney Fei Xizhen stated the case, and filed a lawsuit based on Articles 304 and 305 of the Criminal Law for using violence and coercion to obstruct freedom. When the defendant Gu Changxing was interrogated, he confessed that he had let go of one car and was playing around. No one asked me to let it go. Then the plaintiff Yu Baolong (45 years old, Funing native, i.e., the rickshaw puller whose tires were deflated) testified, saying that yesterday when I was pulling a car through there, there were twenty or thirty people, and they were deflating tires. The defendant came up and pulled a few cars to deflate them. I stopped him and he said, "Don't make noise, or I will drag you to the Chinese territory and kill you." So I reported to the patrolman to arrest him, and the rest ran away. At this point, the court ordered the debate to begin. The police attorney based on the plaintiff's testimony, if the court can trust him, should be convicted according to Article 305 of the Criminal Law, otherwise, judge according to Article 304. The official then questioned the defendant whether he had said any threatening words. Gu Changxing denied saying these words and said that he and four children went to play together, and no adults instructed him. He was asked if there were any relatives at home. He replied that his parents had returned to Jiangbei, and only one brother was doing fish business in the 16th pier. The court verified the confession and immediately announced the verdict in court. Gu Changxing was sentenced to 20 days of detention and a two-year suspended sentence for using violence and coercion to obstruct people's exercise of rights. During the appeal period, the defendant was transferred to the detention center, and during the suspended sentence period, he was handed over to relatives for custody.

How cruel is the way of heaven, and how tragic is the catastrophe for living beings! The association's purpose is to be devoted to fraternity, and its responsibility is to save people. Seeing this hardship, it is difficult to be safe and silent. It is difficult to support a single tree, and it is ashamed to lose the plan of planning. I would like to ask for help from everyone, and I dare to respond to the call of Jiang Bo, not avoiding the criticism of digging a well when thirsty. If the spirit of mutual assistance can save the madness, then human affairs will overcome the sky and save the catastrophe, which will not only be the luck of the disaster victims, but also the blessing of the nation's future. This association cannot express enough its fragrant prayers.

Huaqiang Steamship Had No Communication for Seven Days; There Was a Hurricane in the South Seas; The Company Is Very Anxious 98

In the South Seas, there have been hurricanes attacking for days. There have also been many cases of steamships in Shanghai being attacked by the wind and temporarily anchoring to avoid the wind, or having their electric wires broken by the wind, causing false alarms. Unexpectedly, in this hurricane, the Huaqiang Wheel of Huasheng Company in this port has been missing for many days. Now it is being searched for. The details are as follows:

Shipping Goods from Vietnam

Huasheng Steamship Company recently purchased a giant steamship named Huaqiang, with a deadweight of 5,292 tons. The shipowner is Norwegian. The ship is assigned to sail to the North and South Seas and various places abroad to transport goods and does not carry passengers. This time, it sailed from Shanghai to Annam Haiphong, loaded with passengers and goods, and then went to Hongji to transport coal, and then to Keelung, Taiwan. Unexpectedly, at this time, the ship suddenly disappeared.

Telegram Telling the Voyage

On July 29, Huasheng Company received a telegram from the captain of the Huaqiang Wheel, reporting that the ship had sailed from Haiphong that day and arrived at Hongji. It had loaded all the goods in Hongji. Due to the lack of 500 tons of fuel coal, it set off for Keelung, Taiwan to load coal. Since this telegram, there has been no communication for seven consecutive days. The company is quite worried and decided to send a telegram to inquire.

Whereabouts Unknown

Until the 5th of this month, the company estimated that the voyage should have arrived in Keelung, Taiwan early. Why is there still no news? It immediately telegraphed Keelung to inquire whether the Huaqiang Wheel had arrived in Taiwan, and received a reply saying that it had not arrived in Keelung and its whereabouts were unknown. The company was very alarmed when it received the reply and immediately sent out calls to inquire. Yesterday afternoon, the company asked the Coast Guard to send a telegram on its behalf to call and inquire about the location of all coastal ports and valleys.

Notice to All Parties

Because the ship has peace insurance of 140,000 yuan, and all the crew members, stokers, sailors, etc. also have maritime accident insurance, the company sent a letter to the China Ship Insurance Federation for verification yesterday afternoon. It is heard that the Huaqiang Wheel and its cargo are worth at least 400,000 yuan.

Savings Department Deposits of Jiangnan Bank Decided to Distribute Tomorrow; First Repay All Amounts Under Ten Yuan for One and a Half Years 101

Jiangnan Bank West was unable to operate due to a lack of cash flow, and announced the closure of its Suzhou branch and the simultaneous closure and liquidation on June 5. It entrusted three lawyers, Jiang Yiping, Dong Chi, and Shen Zhaojiu, and three accountants, Shen Jiazhen, Dong Chunbiao, and Jiang Wanping, as liquidators, to handle the liquidation affairs together with the supervisors sent by the Ministry of Finance. Regarding the savings part, there are about 500 savings households, with a total deposit of about 800,000 yuan. However, the amount receivable outside the bank is more than 1.5 million yuan, plus the savings guarantee deposit deposited in the Ministry of Finance, which is enough to pay off all savings deposits. The liquidation office decided to first issue 15% of the savings to the savings depositors from tomorrow, and all debt principals under 10 yuan will be paid off in one lump sum.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Sends a Telegram to the Ministry of Finance Requesting Telecommunications Insurance Policy Stamps; Two Cents Per Thousand Yuan of Insurance Coverage Is No Different From Adding a Business Tax 104

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a telegram to the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing yesterday, which reads: Nanjing Ministry of Finance Junjian, The Insurance Industry Association of this city believes that the stamp tax law will be implemented soon. According to the tax rate table in Article 16 of the law, a stamp of two cents is required for each thousand yuan of insurance coverage, and any amount exceeding one thousand yuan will also be counted as one thousand yuan. The difference between this and the usual stamp duty based on the actual insurance premium collected is huge. The association has directly submitted a request for relief to Junbu on the 2nd of this month. It has been heard that the association has copied the draft submission and sent a letter requesting that we call for assistance. The tax rate table lists insurance policies in Article 14, and although the contract documents in Article 15, the undertaking documents in Article 16, and the joint venture business documents in Article 18 are stipulated to have a stamp duty of two cents for every one hundred yuan, they are all calculated based on the actual amount received. Even though the share capital in Article 17 and the bonds in Article 20 are both taxed at two cents for every one hundred yuan of face value, stocks and bonds are issued at a maximum of 90% of their face value per hundred yuan. The difference is extremely limited. The insurance amount is only a few thousandths of the premium charged for each thousand yuan of insurance coverage. Two cents of stamp duty is the same as two cents of stamp duty for each ten yuan or less. Two cents will be added for each standard exceeded. Comparing this with each other, the stamp duty in Article 14 is actually ten times heavier than those of Article 15 to Article 20. This insurance policy is no different from a contract document in terms of its business relationship, and there seems to be no reason for heavy taxes. If the current tax rate is followed, it is the same as collecting a business tax in advance for those engaged in the insurance business. The same business should not be solely burdened with extremely heavy burdens. Judging from the situation, the formulation of this tax rate at that time was indeed lacking in carefulness. It is reasonable to report the situation to Junbu Jianhe and grant relief within a possible range, which is a matter of public convenience. Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce Kou Yu,

Revitalizing New Industrial Products; Ministry Orders the Use of Chinese Sulfur and Sulfuric Acid; All Factories Should Try Their Best to Match Domestic Products; Order All Transportation Departments to Strictly Manage and Promote Sales 106

The Ministry of Finance issued an order yesterday to the salt and sulfur bureaus of various provinces, the transportation envoys' offices of Yunnan, Sichuan, Guizhou, Gansu, Qinghai, Guangxi, and Shanxi, the Ningxia Trade and Transportation Bureau, the Xinjiang Transportation and Sales Bureau, the Koubei Mongolian Salt Bureau, and the Shaanxi Tax Collection Bureau, saying: Since the Ministry took over the affairs of saltpeter and sulfur, it has made every effort to revitalize domestic saltpeter and sulfur products. For the saltpeter part, there is the Kaifeng Saltpeter Refinery, which purchases hand-made saltpeter and refines fine saltpeter. The potassium nitrate content of this fine saltpeter is more than 99%, which is no less inferior than imported products. It relies on supplying the needs of the whole country, and its effectiveness is gradually increasing. Recently, the affairs of collecting and refining saltpeter in various saltpeter producing areas in the country, such as Xuhai in Ting Su, Caodan in Shandong, 21 counties in northern Anhui, and the entire province of Hebei, have been assigned to the factory for handling, in order to increase raw materials and promote sales. For the sulfur part, the production in Hunan, Hubei, and Henan provinces is the most abundant. They have been repeatedly ordered to improve quality and reduce costs, and to order the provinces to try their best to match them. Recently, an improved sulfur refining test field was established in Xin'an, Henan Province. The latest scientific methods are used to actively improve manufacturing to facilitate sales. Potassium acid has always been supplied by foreign countries, and no domestic manufacturers have manufactured it. The Ministry of Salt Affairs has repeatedly established a Potassium Acid Manufacturing Research Committee to study all matters related to the establishment of potassium acid factories, and has hired domestic industrial experts with rich experience to conduct joint research to promote progress. All of these revitalizations of domestic products are intended to block loopholes and assist industry and commerce, and are also of great benefit to the overall management and increase of tax revenue from saltpeter and sulfur. It is now found that sulfuric acid is also a type of saltpeter and sulfur product, and the number of domestic users is very large. In the past, due to the scarcity of our country's production, most of them were purchased from abroad, and the loss of rights and interests was countless. Recently, domestic acid manufacturing factories, such as Shanghai Kaicheng Acid Manufacturing Company and Tianjin Lizhong Acid Manufacturing Plant, have manufactured sulfuric acid with abundant production. In order to revitalize the national economy, they should be recommended. It is appropriate to order the provinces to immediately comply with this order and transfer it to the factories in the province for use. In the future, when purchasing and transporting sulfuric acid, they must try their best to distribute domestic products. As for how to strictly check the use of sulfuric acid in various industries to emphasize management, and how to effectively promote the sales of domestic sulfuric acid to cultivate tax sources, they should also consider the situation in the province and present it for review and approval. This is the order.

The City's First Batch of Municipal Literacy Schools Ends at the End of the Month; The First Batch of Literacy Schools Will Be Mostly Set Up in Rural Areas; Labor Literacy Schools Must All Be Established Within a Month 107

According to Shanghai News, the municipal government is promoting compulsory literacy education. The first batch of municipal literacy schools will end at the end of this month, and preparations for the second batch of literacy schools will begin immediately. All labor literacy schools must be established uniformly within this month. The details are as follows:

First Batch of Literacy Schools Ends at the End of the Month

There are a total of 220 municipal literacy schools in the first batch. Since school started on July 1, it has been more than a month. The first textbook has been completed at the end of July, and the second textbook is currently being taught. According to the regulations, the time limit is two months and is scheduled to end at the end of this month. The Municipal Literacy Education Committee has sent people to inspect the schools, and the situation is very good. Students who are absent from class for no reason will be punished by the Public Security Bureau, either with fines or hard labor, without any leniency, so there are very few students absent from class.

Second Batch of Literacy Schools Mostly Set Up in Rural Areas

The Municipal Literacy Education Committee believes that July and August are the busy farming season, so the first batch of literacy schools is mostly distributed in urban areas and towns. The second batch of literacy schools will be mostly set up in rural areas because the busy farming season has passed. According to the planned schedule, the second batch of literacy schools will start on September 1 and end at the end of October.

Labor Literacy Schools Must Be Established Within the Time Limit

Regarding the promotion of labor literacy education, the Mountain Literacy Education Committee and the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau have jointly issued a notice requiring all factories, fields, companies, and shops to report the names of literate and illiterate workers in accordance with the regulations. All factories, fields, companies, and shops that should set up labor literacy schools must all be opened before the end of this month. Those who do not set up schools will be severely punished.

It was resolved to nominate Committee Members Chen Tingrui, Yu Chengxiu, and Zhu Fengchi to review the matter; (H) A proposal by Committee Member Xu Zuoliang to negotiate with the First Special District District Court to expand the lawyers' lounge and replace the clock in the Shanghai District Court's lounge. The proposal was adopted; (I) A proposal by Committee Member Xu Zuoliang that members of the Association handling liquidation cases for clients should comply with liquidation principles. It was resolved to nominate Committee Members Wu Guochang, Shen Junru, and Chen Tingrui to review the matter; (J) A proposal by Committee Member Xu Zuoliang that in civil execution cases, in accordance with the First Special District Court's notice, additional execution clerks should be assigned to handle compulsory execution creditors, and special paper should be used for applications to the Civil Execution Office. It was resolved to nominate Committee Members Yu Chengxiu, Zhu Fengchi, and Zhang Shijie to review the matter; (K) A proposal by Committee Member Xu Zuoliang that the Shanghai District Court's delivery of summonses and criminal notices, as well as investigations, are inconvenient for lawyers or parties, and improvements should be requested. It was resolved to forward the case to the Shanghai District Court; (L) A report from Committee Member Shi Lin et al. on the review opinions of member Song Shixiang et al. regarding the establishment of a support association for released prisoners. It was resolved to refer the matter to the Standing Committee for handling; (M) A proposal by member Yao Yongli that various notices from the Association be typeset or lithographed to facilitate review. It was resolved that the matter be filed for future reference, and that the current printing methods of the Association should be further improved; (N) Member Pan Zhensheng sent a letter reporting that his concurrent position as supervisor of the Shanghai United Tug and Lighterage Company did not interfere with his legal practice and requesting permission. Permission was granted; (O) A letter from the Da Ribao newspaper requesting reconsideration of the Association's refusal to allow members to publish title lists and provide positions for exclusive news publications of the Association. It was resolved to file the letter for future reference; (P) The application for membership by lawyers Cao Yongxi and Jin Jiazhang was approved. It was resolved to immediately report the matter to courts at all levels for reference. The meeting adjourned late at night.

Shanghai Chinese Bus Company Adds Twelve New Buses for Use During the National Games 110

The Shanghai Chinese Bus Company anticipates that the upcoming National Games, to be held in the city's central district this year, will draw a large crowd. Concerned that the company's current fleet of vehicles will be insufficient, it has decided to add twelve new buses. The drawings have been submitted to the Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities for approval. For the remaining six buses, the company plans to order 1935 eight-cylinder Ford cars from the Meitong Automobile Company for use at that time.

Epidemic Prevention Work in This City is Tense - No Epidemic has Occurred This Year - Inoculation Work to End Next Month 113

Since the beginning of summer this year, the heat waves in this city have surged at one time. The Municipal Health Bureau has worked extremely hard on epidemic prevention work, so no epidemic has occurred. Now that autumn has arrived, it is hoped that one will not occur. According to an interview with a person in charge of the Municipal Health Bureau, the health authorities of the Chinese and Concession areas in this city during the summer...

Epidemic prevention work... the authorities in charge of health were very concerned with epidemic prevention work. The inoculation teams and disinfection teams worked day and night, with the number of people inoculated reaching over 500,000. The hospitals have not reported any genuine cases of cholera or other seasonal epidemics. The hospitals during this summer were just as busy as usual, without any increase. However, the Municipal Health Bureau has not stopped inoculation work and it is expected to conclude by the end of next month.

Regarding the garbage problem, there was previously a dispute that caused garbage to pile up in the Sixteen Pups area, which was very detrimental to hygiene. The Health Bureau has attached great importance to this issue as it is carrying out epidemic prevention work. Therefore, the bureau has urged the contractors to resolve the problem quickly, and it is now proceeding as normal. The bureau also stated that the transportation of garbage has been inconvenient in the past due to the unresolved pier issue. The Municipal Government has allocated 3,000 yuan to build a dedicated garbage pier in the Sixteen Pups area, and construction will begin soon.

New Zha Sub-bureau Captures Xiang Yixing Kidnappers - Accomplices Confess to Kidnapping Xiang Yixing - Victim Hidden in Dachang has Already Been Moved 114

At about 7:00 p.m. the day before yesterday, Ruan Kaigi, the head of the New Zha sub-bureau in Zhabei, brought in kidnapper Zhu Xiaolong and suspect Huang Miaosheng, who were brought in by Bao Ziying, the leader of the detective team. Ouyang Liu, a member of the bureau, interrogated Zhu Xiaolong, who confessed that he was 32 years old, from Yancheng, currently residing at No. 34 Fenshui Temple Road in Hongkou, and worked in Tao Fen. The kidnapping of Xiang Yixing, the owner of the foundry on Hongnan Shan Road, was initiated by Zhang Hongzhi, also known as Zhang Erlaotouzi. On February 26th of the old calendar this year, he asked me to prepare a boat. I rented a Yang boat from the Gu boatyard in Luodian for a monthly rent of 10 yuan. It was prepared to hide the victim in the boat after the kidnapping, until June 7th, when the boat was taken back due to unpaid rent. On the afternoon of July 20th, I met Zhang Hongzhi in Hongkou, and he told me that the victim had been kidnapped and placed in a duck shed about a mile north of Dachang, guarded by Xiaogouzi and Genbao, who had two pistols. He told me not to talk too much and that I would naturally get my share when the money was obtained. On June 24th (referring to the old calendar), I went to see the duck shed north of Dachang, but Xiaogouzi and Genbao were no longer in the shed and had moved elsewhere. I saw Huang Miaosheng inside. Huang Miaosheng confessed that he was 26 years old, from Dachang, Baoshan County, residing in a bungalow in Hou Xuejiazhai, Dachang, and lived by raising ducks and farming. I did not know anything about Zhu Xiaolong kidnapping, and I do not admit that there was a victim hidden in my house. After the interrogating officer verified the confession, Zhu Xiaolong was found to have admitted to being an accomplice in the kidnapping of Xiang Yixing, so he was ordered to be sent to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation. Huang Miaosheng did not admit to hiding a victim in his house and was released on bail, to be summoned at any time. Yesterday afternoon, Zhu Xiaolong and the confession were sent to the Public Security Bureau for disposal.

Hua Feng Flour Mill Unable to Resume Operations - Social Bureau Approves Legal Layoff of Workers 115

According to the Xin Sheng News Agency, the Hua Feng Xing Ji Flour Mill at No. 289 Yaoshui Lane in West Shanghai was unable to resume operations due to the failure of General Manager Lu Shaotang's real estate business and the resulting bankruptcy. All 320 workers were promised by the factory that they would be paid a living allowance of 8 yuan per month until the factory reopened. For several months, everything was peaceful. But yesterday, the factory announced its closure due to a lack of funds to pay the allowance. The workers negotiated with the factory, and the Social Bureau approved the legal layoff of the workers as the factory was unable to resume operations. However, the factory was ordered to temporarily maintain the workers' living allowance in accordance with the law until the matter was resolved.

All Circles Enthusiastically Participate in Yesterday's Eighth-Eighth National Goods Cigarette Festival - Commemorative Meeting Established - Leaders Express Cooperation - Telegrams Sent to Trade Associations in Various Regions to Rise Up in Unison 116

The National Cigarette Industry has determined August 8th as the Eighth-Eighth National Goods Cigarette Festival. Yesterday, in adverse weather conditions with wind and rain, they still relied on their spirit of unity and, according to the work outline, carried out their work conscientiously, seriously, and with division of labor. For example, major newspapers produced special issues, slogans were posted all over the city, comedy skits were performed in the air, and cigarette factories and stores were specially decorated. The huge publicity effect of eye-catching posters on public buses not only caused a sensation in one corner of the city. At 3:00 p.m., the association held a commemorative meeting at the City Chamber of Commerce, and the ceremony was particularly grand. At that time, the association's standing committee members Yuan Ludeng, Shen Weiting, Shen Xingde, Lao Jingxiu, Jing Yimeng, Ding Houqing, Bao Gengsheng, Wu Linzhi, Sun Daosheng, Ding Zhenbo, and Shen Xuewen cordially entertained the guests. The meeting place was covered with slogans, and the tables were filled with famous cigarettes such as Sanma, Beautiful, Human Life, Guanghua, and Jiabao. Nanyang also presented a pack of White Gold Dragon cigarettes. The meeting ended with refreshments and a photo session. The details of the meeting and the opinions of the newspapers are recorded separately below.

The Grand Occasion of the Establishment Meeting of the Eighth-Eighth National Goods Cigarette Festival (Photo by Changqi)

List of Delegates Present

Yu Zuoting, Wang Yansong, Du Yuesheng (represented by Yuan Ludeng), Chen Zeqing, Zai Boqi, Ma Yinliang, Mi Jifang, Li Haoran (represented by Shen Jicang), Tang Shichang, Guan Jian, Yao Junyu, Wang Jilu (represented by Chen Dafan), Luo Qinghua, Xi Yushu, Hu Xiyuan, Ren Jinping, Xu Xiaochu, Yan Esheng, Wang Xingyao, Zhao Erchang, Jin Runxiang, Zheng Chengqing, Wu Yun Chu (represented by Fang Zhicheng), Zhou Xuexiang, Wang Zhifang, Sun Choucheng and other industry leaders, and representatives from cigarette factories such as Nanyang, Huacheng, Fuxin, Lixing, Huamei, Hexing, Dadong, Ruilun, Cuizhong, Zhongnan, Jiangzhe, etc., including Shen Yankang, Sun Lishan, Wang Gengbao, Hua Weiqing, Zhang Gaonan, Shui Xiangqing, Wang Qiuquan, Wang Xingtang, Shi Xiqing, Han Xushan, and Xi Zhixiang, totaling more than 100 people.

Opening Remarks by the Presidium

Mr. Yuan Ludeng said that today's August 8th Festival has four wishes: first, those who do not smoke should continue not to smoke, but please pay attention to smokers among their relatives and friends, and they must all smoke domestic cigarettes; second, those who already smoke domestic cigarettes should maintain it permanently; third, those who smoke regardless of domestic or foreign cigarettes are requested to recognize that they must smoke domestic cigarettes; and fourth, those who smoke imported goods are requested to switch to domestic cigarettes. Finally, he hoped that starting from "Chinese people should smoke Chinese cigarettes," the goal of "Chinese people should use Chinese goods" could be achieved. Mr. Shen Weiting reported briefly that the domestic cigarette factory has a history of more than 30 years. In these 30 years, it has competed with foreign tobacco in business, and countless people have followed one another. Until last year, there were still more than 40 Chinese factories, but less than half of them could really maintain their business. This year, since foreign tobacco has been competitively priced, the cigarette business has become even more miserable. There have been frequent cases of shutdowns and reduced work. Because there is an organization of the tobacco leaf printing industry, we maintain a spirit of mutual unity and seek common survival and development. Today, we are honored to have leaders from all walks of life participate, which is not only an honor for the future of the cigarette industry, but also the welfare of the entire domestic goods industry.

Speeches by Leaders of Various Industries

(1) Mr. Wang Yansong, representative of the Industrial and Commercial Revival Association, said that today's August 8th Festival can be called the anniversary of the start of the revival movement of your cigarette industry, just like the Revival Association established by the City Chamber of Commerce, which has the same purpose, but one is based on the position of the industry, and the other is a unified planning of various industries. Revival work is like seeking medical treatment and medication, and it is necessary to first understand the source of the disease, and then prescribe the right medicine to achieve practical results. Now, your colleagues in the industry can unite as one, and will surely achieve the goal of common survival and common prosperity in the future. (2) Mr. Chen Zeqing, representative of the City Chamber of Commerce, said that the Eighth-Eighth Festival set by your industry, with the slogan "Chinese people should smoke Chinese cigarettes," all Chinese people should learn from the people of various countries who love their own domestic cigarettes and not haggle over everything. Then this cigarette industry with more than 30 years of history will not be difficult to go from decline to prosperity. (3) Mr. Ma Yinliang, representative of the press, said that whether domestic cigarettes can achieve development depends on the promotion of society and the degree of cooperative efforts of your industry. (4) Mr. Xi Yushu, representative of the financial community, said that the shape of the characters of the Eighth-Eighth Festival has great significance. The upper "eight" character is the first of the "separate" character, and its meaning probably means that the past situation of the domestic cigarette industry has an image of decentralized strength. The lower "eight" character can be regarded as the tail of the "common" character in the phrase "common survival and common prosperity" in your association's purpose, meaning that from today's August 8th Festival onwards, the industry will combine the previously scattered strength into one, and become common survival and common prosperity.

Expressions of the Media

Yesterday's August 8th National Goods Cigarette Festival, the Xinmin, Shen, Chen, Shishi, and Min newspapers in this city all published editorials, either reviewing the causes of past gains and losses of the industry, or specifying the paths to be followed in the future, with far-sighted and thought-provoking words. The association will record them separately and show them as a class of advocacy of the press. (Xinwenbao) Foreign merchants have strong capital and dance with long sleeves, so they can gain an advantage. In addition, social purchasing power is sluggish, and Chinese cigarette factories have been hit hard. Therefore, today we should plan another strategy for maintenance. Also, from the current situation, we should pay attention to two points: first, Chinese cigarette factories should unite as one to seek production and sales cooperation. In this way, we can reduce unnecessary competition and jointly seek the development of the entire industry. The second is to improve technology and goods. There are many reasons why it is not easy to win competition between domestic and foreign goods, and the technical problem is the most important. If each factory can work together and save the cost of unnecessary competition, it will be possible to focus on fundamental issues and stand on the ground forever. (Haoran) (Shenbao) There are three ways for the cigarette industry to save itself in the future. First, to enrich the internal, such as improving the quality of tobacco, improving technology, maintaining integrity, and perfecting the organization. Second, to do solid publicity. Third, to seek production and sales cooperation, so as to avoid the unnecessary waste of competition among the industry. (Du) (Chenbao) The operators of the domestic cigarette industry should strive to promote the realization of production and sales cooperation in the future. Under the cooperation of production and sales, the following effects can be obtained: 1. To avoid the unnecessary losses of competition among the industry. 2. Funds and talents can be concentrated, seeking the progress of technology, and the smoothness of the industry's finances is easy. 3. For the quantity of production, we can have a comprehensive calculation and can have a concentrated force to control the entire market. (Leng) (Shishi Xinbao) If we can follow the principle of self-sufficiency and promote domestic cigarettes, we can also fill a little leak in foreign trade. However, cigarettes are just one of many domestic goods. Today, the industry colleagues can commemorate domestic cigarettes with the August 8th Festival at all costs, which is another posture for the domestic goods movement. For the sake of the entire national industry, we especially hope that other domestic goods industries can follow up and compete directly with the cigarette industry, which is more positive. (Minbao) For the sake of self-preservation of the domestic cigarette industry, the only way out is to abandon self-competition and unite as one. Domestic colleagues have those who unite production and sales cooperation, and the cigarette industry can follow suit. Each factory can use the number of production to allocate sales in various places, eliminating unnecessary competition in the industry. In this way, promotion expenses can be saved, and procedures can be reduced. The savings can be used to improve quality or reduce prices to increase the credibility of the product and suit the purchasing power of consumers. If this is true, the domestic cigarette industry will be enough to talk about survival and resist foreign goods.

Telegrams Sent to Various Regions by the Conference

To the Public Chamber of Commerce of the Cigarette Industry in various places, the recent situation is that our domestic cigarette industry has been greatly affected by the adverse environment, forming a downward trend. Therefore, our colleagues in the association do not want to think about themselves, and are eager to save it. The situation has been reported to the record. Now, in order to expand publicity, hold a long-term perspective, and set August 8th (that is, August 8th) as the National Goods Cigarette Festival, we have specially invited representatives from all walks of life to hold a grand ceremony today. Later, it will be used as an example forever, and we will hold a commemorative meeting on this day every year, shouting loudly, arousing people's deep thoughts, promoting the trend of the establishment, and hoping to achieve the work of lying down and tasting courage. In addition to reporting according to the case, please call on your association to follow the training of everyone and to think about the common feelings of being in the same boat, rise up in unison, support each other, and commemorate it together on this day every year, so that the domestic cigarette business can flourish and gradually reach the bright and splendid field. We hope and pray, the All-China National Goods Cigarette Maintenance Association.

Corpse of a Woman Found in the Huangpu River: The Deceased's Family Background and Life Experiences are Pitiable; The Court is Conducting a Very Thorough Investigation of the Case 117

On the 3rd of this month, when the steamship "Shengjing" of the Daegu Company at Pier 3 of the French Concession was weighing anchor, its propeller churned up the corpse of a woman named Zhang Jinlin, aged 48. The water police brought the body to the Fushe Pier Rescue Bureau, and reported it to the local court, which sent personnel to examine it. The corpse was identified by Zhang Zhou, a relative of the deceased, who arranged for a coffin and burial. Chief Inspector Zhong Shangbin secretly instructed police chiefs Zhang Shuping and Chen Xihui to bring Hao Zhongyang, who was willing to be a witness, and detectives from the water police station to arrest Zhu Fuqing (also known as Chu Fuqing), Qiao Liantang, and Qiao Qi.

These three men and women were immediately brought to the court, where Prosecutor Xie Lian interrogated and detained them for further investigation. The details of this case have been reported in this newspaper. Since the occurrence of this tragedy, the public has been paying close attention. Further investigation has revealed the following: The deceased, Zhang Jinlin, was a local. Her father, who is deceased, served as a comprador for the Yi Feng and Jardine Matheson companies for many years and was quite wealthy. When the deceased married at the age of twenty, she received a rich dowry. Unfortunately, she did not have any children. When she was twenty-nine, her husband passed away from illness. Because her husband's family had few uncles and no children,

her future seemed bleak. Someone arranged for her to remarry to a Mr. Meng, who ran a silk store on Wuma Road. They lived together in a rented house and got along very well. Because they did not have children, they adopted a girl (who is now ten years old and being raised in the Meng family in Shandong). In 1933, the silk store failed, and Mr. Meng had no intention of continuing the business. He sold the store and took Zhang Jinlin and the girl back to his hometown in Shandong. However, Mr. Meng was fond of women. Although he had a wife in his hometown, he also took a 17-year-old girl from Beijing as a concubine, whom he doted on. He treated the deceased like a slave.

Her life was filled with misery. In April of this year (lunar calendar), Mr. Meng ordered the deceased to accompany a relative surnamed Mou to initiate a preaching mission along the Longhai Railway. The deceased took the opportunity to come to Shanghai by boat. She only carried two sets of short shirts and pants, and a rattan suitcase containing two and a half Shandong steamed buns and half a dried lobster. She also carried a gold and diamond ring, and a blue gem-studded ring, a gold watch, and some cash. That was all she had. She had kept her diamond ring and other items closely guarded in Shandong, rarely taking them out. It is said that because she did not have enough travel money, she pawned a jade bracelet for thirteen yuan in the Longhai area, and used two and a half yuan to purchase the aforementioned buns.

She bought a rattan suitcase for storing clothing. The steamed buns and lobster were bought in Shandong to eat along the way. By the time she arrived in Shanghai, the steamed buns were as hard as iron and impossible to swallow. After arriving in Shanghai, the deceased went to the home of her aunt Zhang Zhou at No. 2 Hengde Lane, east of the Xiaoshijie in the city (the deceased was the daughter of Zhang Zhou's elder sister), and stayed there temporarily. The deceased remembered that Chu Fuqing, a Shaoxing native who ran a wooden comb shop in Shanghai, had borrowed 2,000 yuan from her in the past, and a promissory note was made at the time (the promissory note is kept in the Meng family in Shandong). Over the years, neither the principal nor the interest had been paid. Therefore, the deceased repeatedly went to Chu Fuqing

to demand repayment of the principal and interest. Reportedly, he had paid two hundred and sixty yuan several times. The deceased considered it interest, while Chu considered it repayment of the principal. Chu Fuqing also instructed the deceased to publish a statement in the newspaper before he would return the principal in full. Chu Fuqing asked a fortune teller to write a draft for the newspaper announcement, which was published in the Xin Kai Bao’s classifieds on June 6th under the title "Lost Passbook Statement of Cancellation," which stated: (Hereby announcing the loss of a passbook for 2,000 yuan deposited at the Chuyuanxing Wooden Comb Shop west of the Great Hall of the City God Temple in the city. A loss report has been filed with the shop, and the entire amount will be withdrawn. If the passbook is found in the future,

it should be considered invalid. Zhang Lin, signed.) The deceased asked someone to read the draft of the announcement and realized she had been deceived. She then hired a lawyer to file a lawsuit to recover the loan, signing a power of attorney and specifying a legal fee of 440 yuan. While this was in progress, the tragedy suddenly occurred. On the day of the incident, the deceased had dinner at her aunt Zhang Zhou's house. Around 9 PM, the deceased intended to go to the roof of the Xiaoshijie to cool off, but Zhang Zhou, thinking it was cool enough at home, tried to stop her. The deceased replied that she would be back in a moment and left. Unexpectedly, it would be a permanent farewell. That night,

the deceased did not return, but Zhang Zhou did not think much of it. (Zhang Zhou's younger brother, who is the deceased's uncle, lives in the concession and is fairly well-off. The deceased usually stayed at her aunt's house or her uncle's house. However, the deceased's uncle disapproved of her behavior, believing that remarrying after her husband's death was a disgrace to the family. Therefore, although the deceased visited her uncle's house, she did not exchange a word with him.) It was not until the third day that she saw reports in the local newspapers about a female corpse found in the Huangpu River. The description of the deceased's clothing was similar to her niece's. She rushed to the Rescue Bureau to identify the body and confirmed that it was her missing niece. The court is now handling this case with great care and conducting a thorough investigation to ensure that no one is wrongly accused or goes unpunished.

Republican Motor Company: Child Killed by Car; Chauffeur Prosecuted by the Police 118

Yu Yuting, a five-year-old son of Mrs. Yu Dong, a Ningbo native residing at 107 Ou Jia Road, was crossing the road from south to north on the aforementioned road at 3:50 PM the day before yesterday when Xue Yingsheng, the driver of car number 18287 of the Republican Motor Company at 405 Gedeng Road, sped from the east. He could not brake in time and hit the child, knocking him to the ground. The child was severely injured. Upon seeing the accident, Xue immediately took the child to Tongren Hospital in the same car. Due to a refusal to admit the child, he was then transferred to Guangren Hospital. Medical treatment proved ineffective and the child died at 12 o’clock that night. The hospital reported the matter to the Jiaxing Road Police Station, which dispatched detective Feikelun to investigate. The chauffeur was arrested and detained at the police station, and the child's body was taken to the Feilun Road mortuary. Yesterday morning, the police station sent Xue Yingsheng to the First Special District Court to file a public prosecution. As the examination of the body and other matters are still pending, a postponement of the case was approved. At around 10 o'clock, Guo Wei, a prosecutor from the prosecutor's office of the aforementioned court, along with forensic doctor Zhang Yan and clerk Wang Zuyi, arrived at the mortuary to examine the body. First, the western police chief reported the previous situation. Then, Zhang Rongchang and others claimed that they had no family relationship with the deceased. They said that at the time of the accident, they witnessed the car traveling very fast and not honking its horn. After hitting the child, the car dragged him for the length of five storefronts before stopping. At the time, the child was running across the road very fast. When questioned, Xue Yingsheng stated that he was from Nanjing, 28 years old, and lived at 7 Lane 365 Manzhou Road, Zhabei. He had been driving a car for eight years. That day, he was driving at a speed of twenty yards. When he saw the child, he braked and swerved to the north, but it was too late and he hit him. As for not honking the horn, it was because he was driving on a straight road, etc. Prosecutor Guo obtained the statement and determined that the deceased boy, Yu Yuting, had indeed died from injuries sustained after being struck by car number 18287. Since the chauffeur Xue Yingsheng has been publicly prosecuted by the police station, he should await the court's review. The body was handed over to the child’s mother, Mrs. Yu Dong, after she signed a guarantee to take it back for coffin preparation and burial.

Apprentice Falls to His Death 119

At 2:30 PM yesterday, due to the rain, the owner of the Liu Pi Plank Box Store at 24 Lane 488 Tianjin Road, Public Concession, instructed his apprentice Xie Agui (15 years old) to go upstairs to organize the planks stored on the three floors of the building, fearing they would get wet. However, due to the prolonged rain, the ladder was muddy and slippery. Xie accidentally lost his footing and fell to the cement floor below, suffering severe head injuries and bleeding profusely. He was on the verge of death. The shop owner immediately took him to Renji Hospital, but the treatment was ineffective. He died an hour later.

July Work Report of the Municipal Council Legal Department 127

According to the July report of the Public Concession Legal Department, the Municipal Council filed a total of 14,271 lawsuits in the First Special District Court and the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court during that month, slightly more than the 11,751 cases in June. Among these cases, there were 12,994 administrative cases and 1,272 criminal cases. Among the administrative cases, 10,508 defendants failed to appear at the trial and the security deposits paid were confiscated in accordance with the regulations. A total of 2,457 administrative cases were concluded after trial, with 2,449 convicted and 8 acquitted. Among the criminal cases, 5 were dismissed due to insufficient evidence. A total of 1,272 cases were concluded after trial, with 1,084 convicted and 188 acquitted. In total, 3,729 administrative and criminal cases were concluded by the courts in that month, with 3,533 convicted and 116 acquitted. The above figures all show an increase compared to the previous month. In addition to the above public prosecution cases, there were 285 criminal self-prosecution cases. The Municipal Council Health Department and Works Department filed 553 cases. The Traffic Department filed a total of 609 cases for violations of traffic regulations, showing increases and decreases compared to the previous month. Regarding appeals, the Municipal Council filed 2 cases with the High Court. There is still 1 case filed by the Municipal Council that is pending in the Supreme Court, and 1 case in the High Court. A total of 67 appeals were filed by the defendants, including 10 in the Supreme Court, 49 in the High Court, and 8 in the District Court Appeals Chamber. A total of 37 appeals were concluded during that month, including 1 defendant acquitted, 7 appeals rejected, 2 appeals withdrawn, and 27 original sentences reduced. A total of 74 appeals filed by the defendants are pending, including 35 in the Supreme Court, 35 in the High Court, and 4 in the District Court Appeals Chamber. A total of 16 cases requesting the transfer of criminals by authorities outside the concession were received during that month, involving 37 criminals. All were transferred due to sufficient evidence on the surface. As of the end of July, the total number of cases pending in the High Court and District Court was 36, plus 76 appeals, totaling 112 cases. In addition, there were 11 defendants still in custody awaiting trial.

Lin Zeren Invents Copper Plating Method for Glass: A Major Revolution in Thermos Bottle Liners; Ministry of Industry Grants Five-Year Patent 128

The mirror surface on glass is often plated with silver powder, and other substitutes have not yet been invented. Now, Mr. Lin Zeren, a graduate of Soochow University and former technician at the Sichuan Wanxian Tung Oil Inspection Bureau, who has been engaged in chemical research for many years, has painstakingly invented a copper plating method for glass. The color of the mirror surface is brilliant and captivating, like gold. Its reflectivity is stronger than that of silver plating, and its cost is extremely low. In addition to being used for mirrors, this method is most suitable for thermos bottle liners. Most thermos bottles on the market are plated with silver powder. If copper is plated instead, its heat retention ability will be higher than that of silver, and its beautiful color will be very attractive, especially attracting customers' attention. Mr. Lin applied to the Ministry of Industry for a patent for this method, which was approved yesterday. It was passed by the Industrial Technology Review Committee and granted a five-year patent. Those who wish to cooperate with Mr. Lin can contact him at No. 54 Nanjing Road.

Taifeng Biscuit Factory Uses Inventory to Offset Severance Pay 130

The Taifeng Biscuit Factory at 21 Yaoshui Lane in West Shanghai (i.e., the manufacturing plant of the Taifeng Company on Nanjing Road) has a total of more than 150 workers. Since the Taifeng Company was affected by the economic downturn and ceased operations, the workers have repeatedly requested to be laid off according to the law. Wu Xixiang and Others Sue for Embezzlement of 12 Million; Continued Hearing; Defendant Files Counterclaim; Rescheduled to the 13th for Re-hearing 131

Wu Xixiang, Wu Xishu, Wu Xixun, and Wu Xixiu, four brothers currently residing at 22 Puqing Lane, Malan Road, French Concession, and sons of the late Wu Fuqing, the former chief accountant of the Shanghai HSBC Bank from Anhui, previously hired a lawyer and filed a lawsuit in the Criminal Division of the Special Court, accusing their cousin Wu Hengsun, son of the late Wu Youling, the compradore of the Beijing HSBC Bank, residing at 4 Lane 159, Haig Road, of embezzling shared family property and profits from partnership business. The court accepted the lawsuit and held two hearings to summon the defendant. The defendant hired lawyer Chen Yanrui to defend him and filed a counterclaim for false accusation. The court adjourned the hearing and ordered the plaintiffs to invite witnesses to the court for further questioning. Details have been reported in previous newspapers. Yesterday morning, the case was scheduled for a continued hearing. Only Wu Xishao and Wu Xixun, two of the plaintiffs, arrived at the court. The defendant, Wu Hengsun, also arrived with his defense lawyer to await the hearing. At 11:30 AM, Judge Qiu Huanhui presided over the hearing in Criminal Division 2. First, Peng Yuanxun, the attorney representing the plaintiffs, stated that last time he obeyed instructions to bring witness Deng Junxiang to the court for questioning, but now Deng is ill and has gone abroad for treatment, so he was unable to attend today. The judge then questioned Wu Xishao and Wu Xixun about their ages. (Q) Why are the other two plaintiffs, Wu Xixiang and Wu Xixiu, not here today? (A) One has business to attend to, and the other is suffering from a foot ailment, so they did not come. The judge then said that since the defendant has filed a counterclaim, the plaintiffs should all be present, otherwise arrest warrants will be issued. He then questioned Wu Xishao and Wu Xixun on what evidence they had to accuse the defendant of embezzlement. Wu Xixun replied that there were two letters and a statement from a witness already submitted in the case, and that the amount of embezzlement was based on a large portion of the defendant's property and what his late father had said. As for why they had not raised the matter earlier, it was because they were still receiving money at that time. The judge said that these two letters were insufficient to prove embezzlement and asked what they had to say in response to the defendant's counterclaim. (A) We are speaking based on the facts. The judge then asked Wu Xishao if his opinion was the same as Wu Xixun's. (A) The same. The judge then questioned the defendant Wu Hengsun whether you divided the family property. (A) Our ancestors came from Hongyang to escape the disaster. Everyone is self-sufficient. (Q) Was your father's job introduced by the plaintiff's father? (A) No, my father was the only operator of the HSBC Bank compradore, and has nothing to do with the plaintiffs. The judge then gave the letters presented by the plaintiffs to the defendant to read, and the defendant said that the letters were not written by my father. Since there is no seal or signature, how can they be used as evidence? Besides, I know my father's handwriting. (Q) What is the meaning of your counterclaim? (A) They are completely falsely accusing me, so I am filing a counterclaim and requesting a lawful investigation. At this point, the court adjourned the hearing and rescheduled it to the 15th, instructing the plaintiffs to all be present at the next hearing, or arrest warrants would be issued without leniency, and ordered both parties to submit any evidence as soon as possible. After the instructions were given, the court adjourned.
